電影

英國歷史鉅片「鐵腕將軍」 187

上海大戲院今晚九時一刻獻映

英國著名歷史事實「鐵公爵」，現由英國影業巨頭高蒙影片公司耗費萬金製成鉅片，譯名「鐵腕將軍」。特聘英國影壇宿將喬治愛立司第一次在祖國影片中擔任主角，該片因某種關係，被租界當局禁止放映，現由北四川路上海大戲院於四月三十日星期四九時一刻本埠首次獨得放映。該片劇情非常偉大，描述英國名將「惠令登」在「滑鐵廬」大戰的歷史實事，為吳國近年來罕有之出品，亦惟訪院能公映之特殊名片，現已開始定座，屆時預料虬江路北四川路中，車水馬龍，定可轟動一時也。

「浪淘沙」雜寫 188

海濱，無人的孤島，怒濤澎湃，波浪淘着沙磧，當海水洗去後，在沙磧中印跡留着兩個骷髏。

這兩個骷髏，是一對利害衝突下的犧牲者，「浪淘沙」的主題，便由這兩隻骷髏開始。

「浪淘沙」不僅是有着極緊張的戲劇，而且還寫出了一幕人類的大悲劇。

這一幕的悲劇，永存在人類中，不會消滅，人們為了互相的利益，曾暫時携手言和，可是到了各自的利害關頭，他們會立刻翻臉。

「浪淘沙」不但在主題上，是有超乎一切的陳義，在描寫方面，更有特殊的成功，尤其是心理的描寫，可以說體貼入微。

更値得一提的，這是聯華第一部有聲片，而這部有聲片，可以說是真正發揮有聲片功能的一個嘗試。

吳永剛只以「神女」與「小天使」，便奠定了他在藝術界的地位，「浪淘沙」的出現，便是他達到最大成功的階段了。

銀色雜筆 189

月明公司去年好像有大展宏圖的希望，出特刋啦，招股啦，鬧得很不錯的樣子。「昏狂」公映時候，又擴大宣傳，同時從西藏拍得來的風景片，也預備編成一個劇本叫「西藏大觀」。可是沒有多少時候，漸漸的淡了，終於公司無形停頓，職員的薪水欠了好幾個月，一直拖延到現在，看來，恐怕和電通一樣沒有復活的可能了。並且從可靠方面得來消息，任彭年的私人秘書夏天吾已經託張以藩律師追索欠薪了，其他職員也要有同樣的舉動。結果如何，暫時無從得知。

出過一部叫「殘淚」的兆華影業公司，他們曾組織一個歌舞團跑過碼頭，但是賣座慘敗，那部「殘淚」就為了轉押問題，鬧過訴訟。現在那位宣傳員施天，化了胡昂的名字，定於五月一號假大陸商場三樓三百零三號開一個漫畫展覽會。不過他的漫畫與衆不同，是用墨筆畫成木刻的樣子，據他本人說是一種新興的藝術。這幾天施天胡毅昂先生挾了他的得意作品奔走得很忙的樣子。

讀者有閑，明天可以到大陸商塲去一　眼界。

1936.04.30

Hebei-Chahar Anti-Communist Issues: Negotiations Concluded, Chen Zhongfu Ordered to Visit Nagami, Song Zheyuan Banquets Japanese Military Personnel, Continuing to Exchange Opinions 1

(Tianjin) Negotiations on the Hebei-Chahar anti-communist issue have concluded, with only the implementation procedures and mutual exchange of formalities remaining. At 9 a.m. on the 29th, Chen Zhongfu, under orders, visited Nagami to continue discussions. Currently, regarding a certain diplomatic aspect, it has progressed to the stage of canceling the puppet organization in eastern Hebei. The issue awaiting study is personnel matters. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) After a banquet on Haihe Road on the evening of the 29th, Song Zheyuan, accompanied by Xiao Chen, exchanged views with Matsumuro, Nagami, and others regarding the Hebei-Chahar incident, resulting in a more harmonious outcome. Chen Juesheng stated, "I met with Matsumuro today to convey Song's intentions. Judging from the current situation, the differences in opinion between the two sides are minimal, and matters can be resolved quickly." Chairman Song's anti-communist principles remain unchanged. Two meetings have instilled trust in the Japanese side. Xiao Ding will meet with Nagami and Matsumuro again on the 30th for negotiations. Regarding the results of the meetings on the 28th and 29th, the authorities stated that the cancellation of the puppet organization in eastern Hebei has achieved 80% effectiveness, and with another 20% of negotiation, it can be finalized. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) At 7 p.m. on the 29th, Song Zheyuan hosted a banquet at his residence on Haihe Road for Matsumuro, Nagami, Imai, Nakai, and over ten staff officers and military attachés from the Japanese military, accompanied by Xiao Zhenying, Chen Juesheng, Wang Yitang, and Gao Lingwei. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Hamada flew back to Pingjin at noon on the 29th to handle important matters at the Pingjin Special Service Agency. Qin Dechun and Shi Jingting were summoned to Tianjin by Song on the evening of the 29th. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Leaders of China and Japan in North China have been negotiating on "anti-communism" and "eastern Hebei" issues for days. It is reported that the two sides have largely agreed on the results of the anti-communist issue. (29th Hualian News Agency)

(Beiping) Foreign sources report that the Sino-Japanese diplomatic issues being negotiated in Tianjin have taken a sharp turn for the better as of the evening of the 28th. Apart from the Chahar issue, solutions have been agreed upon for both the anti-communist and eastern Hebei issues. However, the timeline for both parties to implement these solutions remains under discussion. In general, the cancellation of the puppet organization in eastern Hebei is no longer a problem. After one or two more rounds of negotiations in Tianjin, the talks can conclude. Qin Dechun was summoned by Song via telegram to discuss crucial public matters in person. He will go to Tianjin with Shi Jingting tonight. Sources related to the matter believe that resolving the eastern Hebei and northern Chahar issues will not be without considerable difficulty. Our side hopes to resolve them together, while the Japanese side advocates resolving them separately. Song plans to return to Pingjin in early June. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sources here received news from Tianjin today that the Sino-Japanese conference held in Tianjin has agreed to cancel the eastern Hebei organization. Xiao Zhenying has already announced this. As for the required procedures after the cancellation, they are currently under discussion. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Hebei-Chahar Diplomatic Committee Internally Divided into Four Groups 2

(Tianjin) Chen Juesheng stated that the Hebei-Chahar Diplomatic Committee was established in Pingjin on the 1st and is internally divided into four groups. The former Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Pingjin has been designated as the committee's headquarters, and the buildings are being renovated. The first matter to be addressed is the Cangshi Railway. As for the allocation of construction funds from the Beining Railway, no decision has yet been made. (29th Dispatch)

Hebei Province: Large Number of County Magistrates Dismissed 3

(Baoding) After examining the county magistrates of Hebei-Chahar, the Political Committee has made appointments and dismissals. He Shaoceng of Wuqing was commended and given a salary increase, while Ding Zhenqing, the county magistrate of Weishui, Anci, and Wuqiao, was transferred to a better position. The county magistrates of Pingxiang, Wanping, Guangping, Guangzong, Wei County, Laishui, Nangong, Jize, Baixiang, Gaoyi, Dongguang, Yanshan, Qingyun, Ding County, Boye, Julu, Ren County, and Shahe, a total of eighteen county magistrates, were all dismissed. Shi Delin, the county magistrate of Jize, abandoned his post without permission and, in addition to being dismissed, was handed over to the Civil Servant Disciplinary Committee for severe punishment. (29th Central News Agency)

Rose's Visit to Kawagoe Involved Two Matters of Inquiry: Obstacles to Smuggling in North China and the Implementation of Currency Reform 4

(Tianjin) External sources report that Li Zi Ross met with Kawagoe on the 28th and raised two matters for inquiry: 1. Smuggling in North China affects British economic interests and causes instability in the Chinese economy. Kawagoe said that the cause of smuggling stems from the excessively high Chinese tariff rates, making it unprofitable to import Japanese goods. Although this is a matter for China as a whole, Chinese merchants have indeed obtained special benefits from Japanese goods. If China corrects the tariffs, it can naturally eliminate smuggling. Li said that he has suggested to the Chinese government to request tax reductions but hopes that the Japanese consul will assist in suppressing smuggling to prevent British merchants' markets from being encroached upon. Kawagoe said that this is a matter for the Chinese government and he has no right to interfere. 2. Li asked about the obstacles to the implementation of unified currency reform in China and what intentions lie behind them. Kawagoe said that he has not heard of such facts as of now. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Liu Zhe visited Sir Li Zi Ross at the British Embassy at 11 a.m. on the 29th, reportedly for a friendly conversation. (29th Central News Agency)

(Tianjin) Japanese newspapers here today stated that Sir Rose, the head of the British economic advisory mission, met with Japanese Ambassador to Tianjin Kawagoe for two hours to discuss the issue of smuggling in North China. Rose stated that the entry of smuggled goods into North China has greatly affected British interests, so he requested that the Japanese take measures to rectify it. Kawagoe replied that smuggling is caused by excessively high Chinese tariffs and cited the smuggling of goods from Hong Kong to Guangzhou to show that smuggling is not limited to one corner of North China. In his reply, Rose hinted that the Chinese government might accept a request to reduce tax rates. Kawagoe had previously served as the Japanese consul in Guangzhou and therefore knew the smuggling situation in Guangdong province in detail, stating that North China is the same as Guangdong province, and the only preventive measure lies in the Chinese customs authorities taking action themselves; Japan cannot interfere. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

North China Flooded with Smuggled Goods, Discussed in British House of Commons 5

(Tianjin) The sales channels for smuggled goods are becoming increasingly congested, with the price of rayon and sugar nearly halved. The total losses of the Japanese ruffians in one week amounted to 100,000 yuan. They are now urgently seeking to open up smuggling routes to the Northwest. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The prices of smuggled sugar and rayon have plummeted in recent days. Tianqiao brand rayon is priced at 87 yuan per piece, Tiantan brand at 92 yuan, and miscellaneous brands at only 80 yuan. Sugar sells for 16.5 yuan per bag. The inventory in a certain concession in Tianjin is increasing daily, and the Japanese ruffians are all complaining. (29th Dispatch)

(London) The serious situation of tax evasion and smuggling in North China was discussed in the House of Commons today. Conservative Party member Chilton asked Foreign Secretary Eden whether he had asked the Japanese government to pay attention to the serious consequences of the large-scale smuggling of Japanese goods into North China through eastern Hebei. What steps will Britain take to secure British loans secured by tariffs? Eden replied that the British government has been paying attention to the serious development of smuggling in North China for some time and has made representations to the Chinese and Japanese governments separately. The British government is now actively considering ways to protect British trade and the security of foreign debts in North China, given the deterioration of the situation and the reduction of tariffs on goods entering North China through demilitarized zones. As for how much China's tariff revenue has been lost, he has not received official news, but the British Embassy in China is expected to send a detailed report to Britain. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Pingjin Military and Police Decide on Preventive Measures for the May Festival 6

(Beiping) The Pingjin military and police authorities have decided on preventive measures to maintain local security due to the many anniversaries in May, with additional police officers being deployed at key locations. (29th Dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang Flies to Taiyuan to Discuss Bandit Suppression with Yan, Chen, etc. Suppressing Bandit Troops Take Encirclement Posture, All Bunkers Have Been Completed, Bandits Fleeing Towards Kangcheng 7

(Taiyuan) Zhang Xueliang, believing that the Jin bandits are collapsing and will likely flee to Shaanxi, has decided to launch a joint attack from Jin and Shaanxi to eliminate them early. This morning, he took a flight from Luochuan and arrived in Taiyuan at 1:40 p.m. The authorities did not receive prior notice. After Zhang got off the plane, he was received by airport personnel and took the airport's car into the city, staying at the reception center, where he met with Chen Cheng and others. Subsequently, Yan Xishan, Xu Yongchang, Yang Aiyuan, Zhao Daiwen, Gao Guizi, and others all visited. Yan scheduled a banquet at 6 p.m. tonight at his official residence. After Yan's visit, Zhang and Chen personally went to Yan's residence to reciprocate the visit, discussing the bandit situation in Jin and Shaanxi at length. (29th Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Our side has changed its strategy against the bandits, deciding to adopt an encirclement posture. All bunkers have been completed, causing extreme panic among the bandit troops. The bandits in Damaijiao and Shuangchizhen, led by Mao bandits, continued to flee towards Kangcheng, attempting to escape the encirclement and avoid being heavily surrounded. Villagers were forced by the bandits in Xiaoyi to lead the way. According to those who escaped, the bandits discussed en route that they are currently surrounded by the National Army and unable to escape. They have been ordered to gather in Kangcheng, preparing to cross the river westward back to Shaanxi. Furthermore, villages along the way have been looted. Yang Chengyuan encountered several hundred bandits on the afternoon of the 27th, who attacked from the direction of Longji and Niaole. After Yang's troops counterattacked, over a hundred bandits were killed, but they were not pursued. (29th Dispatch)

Remnant Bandits in Various Parts of Fujian Can Be Pacified, Yang Weiding Killed Lin Chenghu, Surrendered, Ye Fei Captured Huang Ligui, Gang Collapsed 8

(Fuzhou) The military operations to suppress bandits in this province are making daily progress. The bandits in Yongtai have been cornered after being encircled and suppressed by the garrison. The bandit leader Yang Weiding was killed by the 2nd Security Regiment, and over twenty important bandits were captured alive. Lin Chenghu offered his father as a hostage, requesting permission to reform himself. Ye Fei's remnants of the pseudo-Independent Division of eastern Fujian were surrounded and disarmed in Jianyang, and Ye Fei was captured alive. Huang Ligui's gang of the pseudo-Independent Division of northern Fujian was also forced by the chasing troops to the border of Shouning. The pseudo-8th Regiment in Longyan was annihilated by our Independent 27th Brigade, suffering heavy casualties. The Triad bandits in Datian were also killed by Xie Brigade, with dozens killed. All areas can be pacified in the coming days. (29th Central News Agency)

(Fuzhou) The New 11th Division reported that on the 27th, they captured Ye Fei, the bandit leader on the Fujian-Zhejiang border, and many of his accomplices in Jianyang, and the pseudo-Independent Division of eastern Fujian can be completely annihilated. (29th Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) The remains of officers and soldiers who died in the campaign against the Red bandits were transported to the province on the 28th and will be moved to Chong'an and buried on a scheduled date. (29th Central News Agency)

Li Dijun Denounces Rumors of a Sino-Soviet Treaty 9

(Nanjing) Li Dijun, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Management Department, met with Chinese and foreign journalists on the 29th and made a statement, saying that in recent months, newspapers in Japan and in China have repeatedly published news of China and the Soviet Union signing secret treaties, even fabricating the clauses of the so-called secret treaties as if they were real. Such unfounded rumors have been repeatedly published by the country's newspapers, which cannot but make one suspect that there is another purpose. The duty of newspapers is to report accurately and comment fairly. In this way, they can lead public opinion internally and promote international understanding externally. There is no shortage of enlightened people in the Japanese press. As Sino-Japanese relations begin to be adjusted, it is hoped that they will contribute more to the relationship based on facts. If they are keen to stimulate readers by fabricating facts, it will not only damage the value of their opinions but also easily cause international misunderstandings, which is regrettable. (29th Central News Agency)

Guangdong Steel Plant Construction Contract Signed 10

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong provincial steel plant will be constructed by the British company Baileys, with payment made in installments over six years and construction completed in three years. The contract was signed on the 28th, and construction can begin upon the first installment payment. The future annual output will be 57,000 tons. The signatories were Mr. Lun, a representative of the British company, and Hu Jixian, Qu Fangpu, He Qihan, Li Luchao, and Qian Shufen on our side. (29th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Guangzhou government's steel plant plan has been realized. The contractor for this construction project is the British Blaw-Knox company, with a contract price of 2 million pounds. The contract was signed in Guangzhou today. It is reported that the Nanjing government had given its consent beforehand. It is said that after the plant is completed, it can produce ten tons of copper and iron annually. (28th Kuomintang Telegram)

Wuhan Declares End of Martial Law 11

(Hankou) The police department received an order from the Military Affairs Commission stating that due to the subsiding of the floods, Wuhan can declare the end of martial law. Martial law was lifted on the 29th in compliance with the order, and the Martial Law Commander, Yi Liao Zhong, was also dismissed. (29th Dispatch)

Chiang Flew to Nanchang to Meet with Xiong Shihui, etc., Inspect Municipal Construction; Chiang Convened a Meeting of Representatives from Various Schools in Changsha and Gave a Speech 12

(Nanchang) Chairman Chiang, accompanied by Qian Dajun and his entourage, flew to Nanchang from Hunan on a Ford aircraft on the 29th at noon. Xiong Shihui, Miao Peicheng, and representatives from various party, government, military, and agency organs, numbering several thousand, gathered at the airport to greet him in advance. National flags were hoisted throughout the city. When Chiang disembarked, the welcoming personnel rushed forward to pay their respects, and he returned their greetings one by one. He then went directly from the airport to the official residence to meet with Xiong Shihui and others. He rested at the Lizhi Branch at 1 p.m. and inspected municipal construction at 4 p.m. (29th Central News Agency)

(Nanchang) Chiang flew to Shunwai Airport at 11:30 this morning, where over a thousand people, including military and police officers above the rank of Recommendation, Boy Scouts, and group leaders, welcomed him. He stayed at his former residence in Germany. Chairman Xiong arrived to pay his respects, reporting on the reconstruction after the Jiangxi military and government, and the New Life Movement. The heads of various departments and Zhang Fuliang of the National Economic Council Office then presented their reports and requested instructions in turn. (29th Dispatch)

(Changsha) The Director of Education convened the principals of various schools and students from secondary schools and above to attend a speech by President Chiang at the Yintai Grand Theater at 8 a.m. on the 29th. Approximately 2,000 principals and student representatives from various schools attended, lined up in an orderly manner. When Chiang arrived, the entire audience stood at attention and saluted. He then went on stage to give a speech, which stated that he always has special feelings every time he comes to Hunan. He has especially great expectations for the steadfast, brave, and simple comrades and general youth students in Hunan and deeply believes that in this time of national crisis, Hunan youth certainly have the spirit and courage to turn the tide and can shoulder the heavy responsibility of saving the country and revitalizing the nation and can accomplish the revolutionary cause of standing tall and upright. He hopes that comrades will establish the great ambition of saving the country and the people, emulate the integrity and simplicity of the ancient sage Zeng Wenzheng, the spirit of sacrificing oneself for the benefit of others, cultivate the virtues of filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, righteousness, humility, and shame, unify their will, concentrate their strength, to complete the historical mission of saving the country and revitalizing the nation. Subsequently, Chairman He Jian gave a reply, urging all students to accept President Chiang's instructions with the utmost sincerity and absolutely support the supreme leader. Finally, the meeting was dismissed with slogans. President Chiang drove to the Provincial Party Headquarters for inspection, and all staff members stood silently at the entrance of the Party Headquarters to welcome him. After Chiang inspected the Party Headquarters for a week, he went to the meeting and consulted with the members of the Executive and Supervisory Committees before returning to He Jian's private residence for a rest. (29th Central News Agency)

(Changsha) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek gave a speech to the students at the National Goods Exhibition Hall at 8 a.m. on the 29th, encouraging them to take responsibility for saving the country as young people, to be selfless, and then went to the Provincial Party Headquarters for inspection. (29th Dispatch)

Guizhou Overheated for Days 13

(Guiyang) The city has been extremely hot for days. The meteorological station reported that the highest temperature was 94.5 degrees Fahrenheit. (29th Central News Agency)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Dim Prospect of International Aid to Albania 14

— Heng

Since Italy's war against Albania began on September 25th of last year, eight months have passed in an instant. During this period, the Albanian people relied solely on their flesh and blood and patriotic fervor to resist the Italian army's planes and cannons. Their armaments were vastly different from those of the Italian army, so the outcome was determined before the war even began. The questions were when Albania would surrender and whether the international community could provide Albania with effective assistance in time. Recently, the Albanian army on the northern front repeatedly engaged in fierce battles with the Italian army, which had dense formations and fully mechanized equipment. The resulting heavy casualties accelerated the collapse of the Albanian army. Although the remnants of the Albanian army are still勉力 guarding the highway from Taixi to the Albanian capital, it is doubtful whether they can withstand the Italian army's advance before the rainy season. If the international community cannot immediately put strong pressure on Italy, the fall of the Albanian capital seems to be only a matter of time. However, judging from the current situation, international aid is even more渺茫 than before.

Among the major powers today, the one that relatively has a need to aid Albania is Britain, whose imperial communication lines are threatened by Italy. However, due to complex relationships and excessive considerations, unless it unites with other countries to jointly cope, it lacks the courage to single-handedly undertake the arduous task of suppressing the strong and supporting the weak. British General Robinson stated in his recently published book "On Security" that "There are at least three reasons why my country cannot seek peace: my country possesses great wealth. War only brings losses and no gains; my country's territories are all over the globe, and any area, whether in the air or at sea, is extremely vulnerable to attack, making defense particularly difficult; even if a war breaks out and Britain does not participate, it will at least lose most of its markets and suffer the after-effects of economic collapse." Therefore, Britain can only maintain its prosperity and reap its benefits if the international community is at peace. War is only harmful and not beneficial to Britain. Robinson's remarks can be said to have revealed the British mentality. The reason why Britain supports the League of Nations' collective security policy is also derived from this kind of苟安心理, and the fact that it does not dare to act with independent strength to deal with aggressor nations is also a manifestation of this kind of苟安心理. Last year's Hoare-Laval Pact was indeed an attempt to sacrifice Albania to appease Italy. Although Eden, after taking office, outwardly spoke with strict justice and denounced Italy's aggression, in substance, he did not differ from the Hoare era at all. The reason for this is nothing more than a lack of courageous and enterprising spirit of adventure. At the beginning of last month, Germany suddenly marched into the Rhineland with雷霆手段, and the situation in Europe became increasingly complex, and the possibility of realizing new sanctions against Italy became increasingly impossible. It is even more difficult to expect Britain to provide effective aid to Albania in this situation.

Furthermore, if Britain wants to制意, it must at least obtain France's cooperation. To obtain France's cooperation, it must accept France's views on Germany. However, this will promote the unification of Germany and Italy and make the制意 work even more difficult. This kind of British concern became more and more obvious recently when Germany marched into the Rhineland. France, seeing the ambiguity of Britain's attitude towards Germany, also萌its old habits, showing goodwill to Italy, and causing the Anglo-French cooperation that had just begun to show signs of a turning point. Therefore, unless Britain and France can reach an early compromise on the German issue, Mussolini's military campaign to conquer Albania can be carried out放手直至 Albania's complete surrender. Conversely, even if Britain and France can cooperate effectively on various issues today, it is doubtful whether they can make Italy obey. After Anglo-French cooperation, they have to deal with not only Italy but also Germany. If Germany also emulates what Italy has done, a world war could break out, which Britain is deeply concerned about. Therefore, even if Britain and France can cooperate completely, they do not dare to be too tough on Italy. This can also be inferred.

Now that Albania's resistance to the powerful enemy has reached the point of exhaustion, the international aid is becoming more and more渺茫. How can we expect the League of Nations' institutions not to be damaged and the arrogance of aggressor nations not to be raised?

Legislative Yuan 24-Member Committee Passes National Assembly Election Representative Quota; Legislative Yuan to Review Organizational Law Today, and Important Draft Constitution Bills Tomorrow 15

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan's 24-member committee held its fourth meeting on the morning of the 29th, chaired by convener Fu Bingchang. It passed all the reserved clauses and appendices in the first draft of the National Assembly Representative Election Law concerning the distribution of representative quotas. A preliminary review report has now been drafted and presented to the Yuan for review along with the draft law. The committee's drafting of the two National Assembly laws is now temporarily completed. Due to the large number of bills this week, the Legislative Yuan has decided to advance this week's Yuan meeting to 9 a.m. on the 30th to continue reviewing the National Assembly Organization Law and the Amendment to the Executive Yuan Organization Law. The Yuan meeting will continue all day on the 1st to review important bills such as the Draft Constitution and the National Assembly Representative Election Law. The details of the final drafting and decision-making regarding the distribution of representative quotas in the National Assembly Representative Election Law are recorded below: Provincial Regional Representatives: Jiangsu 44, Zhejiang 33, Anhui 35, Jiangxi 28, Hubei 40, Hunan 43, Sichuan 44, Kangding 9, Hebei 43, Shandong 44, Shanxi 22, Henan 44, Shaanxi 20, Gansu 14, Qinghai 9, Fujian 22, Guangdong 44, Guangxi 21, Yunnan 22, Guizhou 16, Chahar 10, Suiyuan 10, Ningxia 9, Xinjiang 12. Municipal Regional Representatives: Beijing 4, Shanghai 8, Beiping 6, Tianjin 5, Qingdao 2, Xijing 2, totaling 665. Vocational Elections: Provincial and Municipal Vocational Organizations: Jiangsu 21, Zhejiang 15, Anhui 15, Jiangxi 18, Hubei 18, Hunan 21, Sichuan 21, Kangding 3, Hebei 21, Shandong 21, Shanxi 8, Henan 21, Shaanxi 11, Gansu 5, Qinghai 3, Fujian 9, Guangdong 21, Guangxi 7, Yunnan 8, Guizhou 7, Chahar 3, Suiyuan 3, Ningxia 3, Xinjiang 3, Beijing 6, Shanghai 12, Beiping 6, Tianjin 6, Qingdao 3, Xijing 3. Liberal Professional Organizations: Lawyers 10, Accountants 5, Medical Practitioners 8, Journalists 11, Engineers 6, Educational Associations, National Universities, Independent Colleges, Teacher Organizations of Universities and Independent Colleges Registered with the Ministry of Education, 8 each, totaling 380. Special Elections: Northeast 45, Mongol and Tibetan (Mongol 24, Tibetan 16), Overseas Chinese in Malaysia and Siam 5 each, in the Dutch East Indies 4, in Annam 3, in the United States, Canada, and Burma 2 each, and 1 each in the rest, totaling 45. Military: 30, totaling 1,200. (29th Central News Agency) The 58th meeting of the fourth session of the Legislative Yuan was decided to be changed to 9 a.m. on the 30th. (29th Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) At the Legislative Yuan's plenary meeting on the morning of the 30th, in addition to continuing discussions on the National Assembly Organization Law, the Amendment to the Executive Yuan Organization Law will also be discussed. A regular meeting will continue to be held on the 1st to continue discussing the Amendment to the Draft Constitution. (29th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The National Assembly Representative Election Law has been completed and submitted to the central government. According to Fu Bingchang, convener of the 24-member committee responsible for supervising the election, the Representative Election Law consists of a total of 62 articles and four appendices. The quota distribution section was revised based on the principles handed down by the central government. Representatives from the Northeast provinces have been increased. A general supervisor will be set up in the central government during the election. Vocational elections and special elections will each be supervised by the central government's competent authorities. Regional elections in each province will be supervised by the Director of Civil Affairs. The distribution of regions in each province is based on the existing administrative inspectorate area as the standard. In areas where no inspectors have been set up, the old prefectural areas will be used. Where a part of the old prefectural area has been划入 into the inspectorate area, the Ministry of Interior and the provincial governments have discussed and stipulated the rules. Vocational organizations should participate in vocational elections and may not participate in provincial and regional elections. Among special cities, Shanghai has the largest population, with eight representatives, and Nanjing has a slightly smaller population, with four representatives. (29th Dispatch)

The Mongols have no choice but to recall their children who have been sent to Lama temples to raise livestock. There are many Japanese living in Prince Teh's mansion near Pangjiang, and hundreds of Mongolian soldiers under Li Shouxin are also stationed in Bailingmiao. The Japanese are making every effort to have Mongolian foreign trade pass through Dolon, instead of going south to mainland China. Tax checkpoints have been set up in places like Zhangbei, controlled by the Japanese, to control everything. Japanese merchants are now importing American freight vehicles from Dalian into Inner Mongolia, and their selling price is 450 yuan cheaper than those transported to Inner Mongolia via the Ping-Sui Railway. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Jiang Tingfu Discusses Reforming Local Administration: Sound Organization Utilizes Talent to Its Fullest 19

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan has recently been paying close attention to the investigation of the work of its subordinate agencies, the evaluation of job responsibilities, the adjustment of functions, and the general reform of local administration. A reporter recently visited Jiang Tingfu to inquire about the central government's strategy for reforming local administration. According to his statement, sound administration is nothing more than: compact organization, flexible operation, appropriate powers, suitable talent, talent utilized to its fullest, and sufficient funding, rationally allocated. China's local governments are far from sound in these three aspects. He believes that there are several points that should be improved: In recent years, the central government and the Provisional Headquarters have implemented many new measures, such as joint offices, the establishment of commissioners, and the transformation of county government bureaus into sections, which have been vigorously promoted. However, there are still many problems to be solved, and President Jiang is paying close attention. At present, county governments lack sufficient funds for administration, and there is no talk of funding for undertakings. However, the county governments are required to carry out more and more undertakings, leading them to regard county administration as a daunting task and gather in senior agencies to engage in the transfer of official documents, making administration increasingly hollow. The functions and powers of administrative commissioners should not be limited to liaison between superiors and subordinates, and should be clearly defined and analyzed. Local security is the foundation of all kinds of construction. Those who maintain public order in various places include the police, defense corps, troops, and baojia, etc., which cost the people a great deal of money, but the results are very low. The reason why the people become bandits is mostly because they are forced by livelihood and take risks. In short, to make reforms effective, one must recognize the problem itself and prescribe the right medicine, so as to avoid changing orders in the morning and evening, and making things more complicated. The purpose of the Executive Yuan convening a meeting of commissioners is to listen to opinions and solicit expert advice, and personnel will be sent to inspect after the meeting to understand the crux of each problem, in order to obtain a simple and easy-to-implement improvement strategy. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Liang Han Cao and Others Study Reviving the Rural Economy: Revising the Outline of Cooperative Business Organizations, Etc., with Separate Regulations for Central and Local Organizations 20

(Nanjing) Sun Ke previously planned to comprehensively coordinate the revitalization of the rural economy with the strength of the government based on cooperative principles, and ordered Liang Han Cao and more than ten legislators to study concrete implementation measures. Now the first step has been completed, and on the afternoon of the 29th, a meeting was held inviting Liang Han Cao, Ma Yinchu, and others, and the method of organizing or systematizing cooperative businesses was passed. The rest regarding the implementation procedure will be decided in a follow-up discussion. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ma Yinchu Discusses Opinions on Reviving the Countryside: Future Rural Loans Should Be Unified, and Bank Interest Rate Reductions Should Be Carefully Considered 21

(Nanjing) Ma Yinchu, the Chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, shared his views on the plan to revive the countryside, as well as the influence of Li Ziluosi's recent speech, and also discussed the issue of bank interest rate reductions. Ma said that well-known figures in the domestic economic circles currently have differing opinions on the economic decline of society in recent years. Some advocate reviving the countryside, while others advocate revitalizing industry, each with their own reasons. He believes that without reviving agriculture, the economy of farmers will not recover, and the purchasing power of the majority of the population, the farmers, will still not be able to increase. Therefore, reviving agriculture should be the priority, but revitalizing industry should not be neglected either. This is a matter of sequence, and there is no difference in importance. At present, the best cooperative societies in the country are those organized by the China International Famine Relief Commission, Zhang Yuanshan, and others. Their organization is from the bottom up, ensuring that the organization is sound and the members are pure. Although there are many cooperative societies in other places, they are not very sound. It is necessary to train and guide talent, detach from urban life, and personally go to the countryside to make farmers understand the benefits of cooperation, and to increase the cost and benefits of individual production, then it can be promoted unimpeded. As for the current separate investments of various banks in rural areas, much of it is actually lost. This type of cooperative society aims to provide loans, and the investments of various banks are not the same. As a result, a cooperative society can obtain loans from several banks. Therefore, the use of loans, whether they are for agricultural affairs, cannot be proven. Ultimately, the loans cannot be repaid, affecting the credit of the cooperative society. In the future, it is necessary to unify rural loans. As for income tax and inheritance tax, they are good taxes. The current tax rates in our country are all levied on ordinary people, and consumption tax is also a transfer tax, which is borne by users, regardless of rich or poor. Only those who own assets and deposit money in banks are not taxed, which is very unfair. Therefore, income tax and inheritance tax are taxes levied on the rich. As for the legislator Xiao Shuyu's proposal to monopolize salt, once this tax rate is implemented, the livelihood of ordinary people will be further increased. I personally do not want to agree. Furthermore, Sir Li Ziluosi's recent opinions in Shanghai on Chinese finance are helpful as suggestions from others. However, regarding the section on inflation mentioned by Luo, there is no such fact in China's current finances. Ma also said that the general public advocates that banks reduce loan interest rates, and the central bank should consider ways to deal with the economic situation on the market. However, the reduction of bank loan interest rates also means the simultaneous reduction of interest rates on deposits. Currently, foreign banks in China are raising deposit interest rates to 6% or 7%. If domestic banks reduce deposit interest rates, there is a risk that capital will flow into foreign banks. This should be carefully considered. (29th Special Dispatch)

Lu salt exported to Japan should meet the needs of Japanese industry and must not be used as edible salt. This layer requires the guarantee of the Japanese government. After Lu salt is exported, the Japanese side must not import it back (because the people of our country must bear national tax and local surcharges for edible salt, totaling eight yuan per dan. Prevent the Japanese side from re-importing it after exporting it, which is called inverting). These measures stipulate that the four places of Changlu, Lianghuai, Shandong, and Fujian can all be applied. On the surface, the tax rate required by the government is reduced, but the exports can replenish the revenue and at the same time increase sales and reduce smuggling. (29th Special Dispatch)

League of Nations Committee Unanimously Passes Our Country's Semi-Permanent Council Seat Case: Term of One Year, Re-election Not Restricted 26

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council Organization Committee continued to discuss China's request for a semi-permanent council seat tonight. After three hours of debate, it passed the report drafted by Lord Cecil and adjourned. The committee unanimously approved China's return to the Administrative Council. However, regarding the term issue, it was believed that if the term was set at one year, there would still be the right to be re-elected after the one-year term expired, without the usual restriction on consecutive re-election. Mr. Cecil's report was drafted based on this principle and will be distributed to all parties tomorrow. Our representative Guo Taiqi and Lord Cecil are scheduled to return to London tomorrow night. (28th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council Councillor Quota Allocation Committee decided yesterday to submit recommendations to the Administrative Council and the League of Nations General Assembly, advocating that a temporary council seat should be added for China. Well-informed sources believe that the Administrative Council and the General Assembly will definitely pass it when they discuss this case in the future. It is understood that the committee has been meeting since the 27th of this month to discuss two principled issues: Should the Administrative Council add a council seat, and how long should the term of the newly added council seat be? Regarding the first issue, although the representatives of Sweden and Canada expressed dissent, the committee still decided to add a seat and give it to China. Since Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, there has been no Asian representative in the Administrative Council. Now that the Chinese government has made a request, it should naturally be given to that country. As for the temporary council seat added in 1933, which was given to Portugal, it should still be maintained. Then the issue of the term of the newly added councillor was discussed. The representatives of France, Spain, Argentina, Romania, and Italy all proposed a term of one year. The British representative, Lord Cecil, advocated that the usual term of three years for semi-permanent councillors of the Administrative Council should be followed. At that time, the voting result was that nine countries supported the British proposal. In addition, the representatives of Poland and Canada both waived their voting rights. Once the three-year term of the councillor added in 1933, that is, the seat given to Portugal, expires, it should still be given to European member states. It is expected that there will be many contenders for this seat, including Latvia, Austria, and Portugal, who are expected to make demands. (29th Havas Dispatch)

At the same time, it can also show the German Fascist Party's fervor for war preparation and its ambition for aggression. (TASS dispatch, 29th)

(Berlin) The government issued an order yesterday granting Air Minister General Goering broad powers, entrusting him with all matters relating to raw materials and foreign currency, making him in practice the "supreme dictator" of the German economy. After the issuance of this order, various industrial stocks fell on exchanges across the country. It is generally believed that the position of Economics Minister Dr. Schacht is obviously affected. Although the government gazette stated that Goering's new position was to enhance Schacht's political position, economic circles did not dare to believe it, and believed that Schacht had delivered a speech in Königsberg on August 18 last year, expressing his opposition to the National Socialist Party's anti-Jewish movement. Since then, the radical elements of the National Socialist Party have attacked Schacht, leading to a fierce storm. Until recently, the mutual attacks have reached their peak. The government's granting of broad powers to General Goering is actually a natural result. Schacht was originally not a member of the National Socialist Party, but he was rich in experience in financial and economic matters. The National Socialist Party government relied on Schacht's assistance in increasing economic activity, building automobile roads, organizing public works, and reforming armaments. Therefore, it borrowed his talent, but the radical elements in the party have always criticized Schacht for his liberalism and attacked him at every turn. For example, Kepler, Hitler's confidant and party spokesman, had demanded his dismissal three months ago because Schacht's views on various major issues (such as the anti-Jewish movement and the policy of economic self-sufficiency) differed from those of the party. In addition, Minister of Agriculture Dahl was also incompatible with Schacht. Schacht urgently wanted to restore Germany's foreign trade, while Dahl advocated a policy of economic self-sufficiency so that Germany's food supply would no longer depend on foreign countries. The situation of conflict between the two parties can be seen in Schacht's letter to Dahl at the time (Dahl insisted that Germany must be self-sufficient in meat and fats, and Schacht replied with a letter, which was recently leaked by well-informed sources). The content roughly stated, "I am not a magician and cannot turn stone into gold. At this time, the most important issue in German agriculture is to restore agricultural output based on the figures for 1933." Recently, the National Socialist Party's opposition to Schacht has suddenly intensified due to the increasingly exhausted sources of raw materials and foreign exchange in Germany. For example, a large textile factory in Leipzig issued its annual report yesterday, which stated that the sources of supply for wool, iron ore, coal oil, tungsten, manganese, leather, etc., may be exhausted next year. The importance of the raw material problem can be seen from this. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Southern Front: 5,000 Ethiopian Troops Counterattack at Night; Brave and Skilled Italian Troops' Attack Thwarted; Heavy Rain and Mud Render Motorized Units Useless; Sassabane Remains in Ethiopian Hands 39

(Gorahai) 5,000 Ethiopian soldiers launched a sudden counterattack last night, exerting significant pressure on the camps and headquarters of the Italian Blackshirts here, causing many visitors to experience the flavor of war. The situation was very dangerous at one point, as Ethiopian soldiers fired artillery shells at the Italian camp, setting fire to the bushes. The gasoline used by the Italian army's motor transport team was stored in the bushes. Reuters special correspondent Captain Barnes was writing a telegram in a heavy truck when bullets rained down. Two people in the vehicle were killed and six were injured. Everyone in the camp was ordered to defend themselves. Fortunately, a large unit of soldiers from Somaliland bravely resisted the repeated attacks, followed by bayonets and hand grenades, directly attacking forward, and finally driving the enemy across the Fa Fang River. Ethiopian soldiers abandoned 600 bodies on the battlefield. When these people were strafed by machine guns, many people were still fighting frantically in the chaos. Ten Italian officers were killed and twenty-three were injured. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

(Rome) Italian Army Commander General Graziani on the Southern Ethiopian Front, due to heavy rains on the front line and his troops' exhaustion from three days of fierce fighting, has ordered a temporary halt to the offensive. Heavy rain is pouring down on the entire front line, and roads have been flooded. Engineers are currently building bridges day and night at the confluence of the Fa Fang River and the Chia Riel River. A 120-foot-long bridge was built over the Fa Fang River in two hours today. The Italian army is currently encountering strong enemies, and their bravery is truly unexpected. Therefore, the plan to capture Sassabane has not yet matured. According to news from Dire Dawa, the Sassabane battle, which began three days ago, is still in full swing. Ethiopian soldiers are fighting to the death, repeatedly defeating the attacking Italian army. The Italian army is currently transferring reinforcements from all sides to fight. According to official news, the Italian army attacked Sassabane and engaged in a fierce battle with General Nasibu's Ethiopian army, suffering heavy losses. Twenty-one white officers were killed and eighteen were injured. Twenty-seven white soldiers were killed and forty-seven were injured. 1,367 enlisted soldiers were killed. At the same time, thirteen Italian army planes were hit by Ethiopian army anti-aircraft guns, and five pilots were injured. It is said that the Ethiopian army led by General Nasibu possesses modern weapons, has received rigorous training, is brave and skilled in battle, and the number of soldiers far exceeds that of the Italian army. (National News dispatch, 29th)

According to them, they are now returning to the capital on government orders and plan to go to the front line again in the future to continue fighting. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Egyptian Young Monarch Accedes to the Throne; New Monarch Returns Home Today from London; Three Regents to Handle State Affairs 41

(Cairo) After the death of King Fuad I, the cabinet held a meeting yesterday to announce that Crown Prince Farouk would succeed to the throne, and issued a bulletin stating that the current King Farouk is scheduled to depart from London on a British mail ship at 1:50 pm on Thursday (30th), and will pass through the port of Marseille, France on May 1st, and arrive in Egypt on May 5th. The cabinet meeting also decided to hold the House of Representatives election on May 11th, because when the Crown Prince accedes to the throne at a young age, a regency council must be formed within ten days of the death of the late monarch to attend the House of Representatives. The regency council will be composed of three regents, appointed by the late monarch in his will before his death, which is sealed and will be opened only when the House of Representatives is convened. In addition, the issue of reconvening the Senate is the key to the political situation, because when the 1923 constitution was abolished in 1930, the Senate was also dissolved. Now that the constitution has been restored, the Senate should also be reconvened to meet, which is the correct way to handle it. However, according to this newspaper's reporter, although the Kuomintang's view is as such, there are practical difficulties and it may not be possible to do so. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

(Cairo) Egyptian Crown Prince Farouk will ascend the throne when he arrives in Cairo from England on May 5th, but because he is still a minor, the regency council will act as his agent in political affairs. The Crown Prince stayed in England for six months and is scheduled to leave London tomorrow for Marseille, taking the British Company's mail ship Indupugna home. The ship will specially dock temporarily in the port of Alexandria to allow the Crown Prince to disembark. The British Emperor personally offered condolences to the Crown Prince yesterday and ordered mourning for King Fuad for seven days from today. The Egyptian general election will still be held on May 2nd and will not be postponed due to the king's death. The cabinet has not yet decided who will act as the monarch's agent. According to Egyptian customs, women are not allowed to govern, so the Crown Prince's four sisters have no hope. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

(Cairo) One of the main reasons for King Fuad's death was a bullet he suffered 30 years ago. The king was not yet on the throne at the time. One day, while sitting with politicians and diplomats playing chess in a large club in Cairo, his brother-in-law, Prince Saif al-Din, suddenly arrived and shot him, the bullet piercing his throat. Although he recovered after treatment, he often suffered from choking coughs, so when this disease broke out, he first suffered from blood disease. In addition, the king had been suffering from heart failure for nearly 20 months, which led to his death. When the king was critically ill, seven doctors injected antiseptic fluid into him from time to time, causing him great pain. The king then said to the doctors, "Why don't you let me die peacefully and avoid the pain?" (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Brief History of the New Monarch Farouk 42

Egyptian Crown Prince Farouk was born in Cairo on February 11, 1920. His father Fuad attached great importance to his education, hoping that he would become a useful person. He once said to others, "What is the value of being a Crown Prince? Only a useful person has value." Therefore, all of Farouk's toys when he was young were of an educational nature. When he grew up, he liked to read, collect stamps, take photographs, and was fond of sports. He was fluent in English and French. At the age of 15, he went to England to study, preparing to enter the Royal Military College of England in two years. His height was above average, his appearance was upright, and he was proficient in etiquette. When he took a warship from Alexandria to Port Said, the crew saw him waving a white towel to signal to the shore. The crew was surprised and asked why he was waving the towel since he was far away from the palace and people could not see him. Farouk replied that before he left, he had placed a telescope in the palace and he thought his sisters were holding telescopes to watch him from afar, so he waved the towel to say goodbye to them. After arriving in England, he hired teachers to study various subjects, preparing to enter military college at the age of 17. In 1933, he was named Prince of Upper Egypt. He participated in domestic celebrations on behalf of his father and also served as the head of the Egyptian Boy Scouts that year. He was quick-witted and well-informed about world affairs. (Reuters)

Hebei-Chahar Authorities Discuss Anti-Communist Agreement with Japanese

Beiping Correspondence: Since the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, the situation in North China has been under constant pressure from the Japanese. However, diplomatic negotiations have not ceased. Song Zheyuan, who bears the heavy responsibility of managing the situation, has repeatedly stated to the people of North China that, while striving for good neighborly relations, he does not want to lose sovereignty and dignity. However, the Japanese view of North China is to establish a special regime detached from the central government, leaning towards so-called genuine cooperation among China, Japan, and "Manchukuo." Therefore, their diplomatic tone inevitably clashes with our desire to maintain sovereignty and dignity. The major issues in North China's diplomacy are the Hebei-East problem and the Chahar-North problem. Intermittent negotiations have been ongoing for half a year. At the beginning of the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, Xiao Zhenying repeatedly negotiated with Doihara Kenji of the other side in Pingjin, but ultimately failed to reach an agreement. After Doihara Kenji returned to Japan, the negotiating party changed to the Japanese garrison authorities in Tianjin. Although it was relatively smooth for a time, the February 26th Tokyo Incident occurred. Nagami Toshitoku, the chief of staff of the Japanese army in Tianjin, returned to Japan for instructions but received no results. As the anti-communist problem in North China became pressing, Sino-Japanese diplomacy in North China inevitably became tense again. As a result, the negotiations between Xiao Zhenying and the Japanese side became active again. Nagami Toshitoku twice returned to Japan for instructions. After returning to Tianjin, he met with Xiao Zhenying twice on the 20th of this month. There were various rumors from the outside world, saying that the negotiations had resulted in all concrete decisions. In reality, the problem is not as easy to solve as rumored.

Song Zheyuan believed that the anti-communist agreement concerned the national system and did not dare to act arbitrarily. He telegraphed the Japanese demands to the central government for instructions on how to handle them. In recent days, private negotiations between Xiao Zhenying and Nagami and others have reportedly become closer. On May 1st, both China and Japan will officially begin negotiations in Tianjin. Song Zheyuan must wait until the diplomatic problems have made some progress before he can return to Beiping and has stated that once the diplomatic problems are resolved, he will announce the situation to the world to dispel suspicion. However, general observations suggest that the diplomatic situation in North China is too complex, and it is feared that it will be difficult to reach a resolution in the short term. (28th)

Communist Bandit Forces in Northern Shaanxi are Weakening

Only a Few Remnants Remain

Russian Litov Remains to Oversee

Hope is Lost After the Death of Bandit Du

Taiyuan Correspondence: After the Communist bandits decided to cross the Yellow River from northern Shaanxi to disturb Shanxi, they were severely suppressed by the National Army. The bandits disintegrated and fled in two directions, north and south. This has been going on for two months. Moreover, the Shanxi-Suiyuan Army, the Central Army, and the Shaanxi-Henan armies are defending in separate areas and attacking from the north and south, and the bandit forces are weakening. According to recent intelligence reports, the bandits, in their desperate state, are planning to return to Shaanxi. Therefore, recently, the remnants of all routes have been concentrated in the Zhongshi area of western Shanxi. However, the Shaanxi army has deployed defenses along the river to prevent the bandits from returning. It is thought that the bandits will not easily return. After the Communist bandits entered Shanxi, the bandit forces in northern Shaanxi are not as strong as before. Mao Jizhai, the political commissioner of Yulin, Shaanxi, has come to Taiyuan to visit Yan and personally report on the recent situation in northern Shaanxi, so that the National Army can accurately assess the bandits. The main points of Mao's report are as follows:

North of Jia County and east of Yulin, there are only the bandit forces of Wang Zhaoxiang and the remnants of Liu Zidan's troops in Shaanxi, only about six or seven hundred men.

In Sanbian, there are Liu Jinfan's (Liu Zidan's younger brother) bandit troops, 500 infantry bandits, and 300 cavalry bandits.

In Hengshan, there are 500 to 600 bandits from Niu Gang.

North of Wubao, there is Liu Zidan's newly formed battalion of 500 to 600 men, with only 100 rifles. The bandits who crossed the river from Yu County came from the Shaomao Tou opposite Luoyu Kou, about 1,000 men. It is confirmed that they were the troops of Liu Zidan and Xu Haidong who joined forces and fled south. In Jijiayuan, Zhongyang, they were attacked by Fang Brigade Zhang Tuan of the National Army. Bandit Liu Zidan was seriously injured and has returned to Yongping Town, Yanchuan, northern Shaanxi, for treatment.

The remaining bandits in northern Shaanxi have rifles for less than half of their number, and the bandit forces are greatly weakened. Currently, only Xu Yubo (Chinese), Litov (Russian) are overseeing near Wazi Fort, with 500 to 600 Red Army soldiers and a Red Army school. Recently, because the bandits who crossed the river to disturb Shanxi suffered too many casualties and it was impossible to recruit replacements, Liu Zidan's pseudo-chief of staff, Du Wenchang, was appointed as the commander of the new division and tried his best to recruit in the hope of replenishing the various combat bandit troops. However, bandit Du was killed by the cavalry of Gao Guizi's division a few days ago and his head was displayed. Moreover, the military affairs of the Communist bandits in northern Shaanxi mostly relied on bandit Du. After his death, not only was the morale of the remaining bandits in northern Shaanxi greatly affected, but also the hope of replenishing the bandit troops fleeing to Shanxi has been dashed. (April 27th)

Han Fuqu Appoints Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau

Summons all General and Sub-Section Chiefs for Instructions

Jinan Correspondence: Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, resigned due to illness. Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Provincial Government, decided to concurrently serve as the Director of the Bureau because this year's river defense is more difficult than last year. Han decided to concurrently serve as the Director of the Bureau and personally supervise the staff to work hard to defend the river and ensure safety. Zhang Lianjia ordered the various departments and offices of the Bureau to handle the handover last Thursday. Han also ordered all general and sub-section chiefs within the province to come to Jinan to receive instructions. At 7:00 AM on the 27th, Han sent Hou Xitian, Li Yuying, Bian Chongxiu, and Qiu Zhen to the River Affairs Bureau. Hou took over the accounting, Li was responsible for checking all the staff, Bian took over engineering affairs and was responsible for drawing detailed maps, and Qiu handled agricultural and forestry affairs (because the dikes along the river are very long and there is a lot of land, Han wants to develop agricultural and forestry affairs). The handover was completed that day. The former director Zhang Lianjia, along with the general and sub-section chiefs from the upper and lower reaches, the section chiefs of the three sections of the Bureau, the director of the industrial and electrical bureau, and others, went to the Provincial Government to meet Han in the Provincial Chairman's office. Han gave a sincere speech, which lasted for an hour. The main points of his speech were: "I have decided to summon everyone for instructions on a few points. Regarding the breach last year, I feel very sad when I bring this up. The director of the bureau at the time should take responsibility, and you should also take a great deal of responsibility. The breach should not have been a problem. When the water is high and the current is strong, it is difficult to exert force. Just like using troops, victory and defeat are uncertain. Preventing floods is like defending against the enemy. If a breach occurs before taking measures to prevent it, then everyone is to blame." (Speaking to this point, he asked the people around him what the punishment was for breaches in the Qing Dynasty. The people around him replied that all civil and military officials were dismissed and allowed to work, and they would be reinstated after the breach was blocked.) "Regarding the Yellow River, the Central Government has established the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission to make overall plans. Although the provinces are still responsible for defense, they must listen to the Central Government's instructions. What I am telling you today is that you must prevent another breach and also look at the results of the tree planting. It must be neat and tidy, looking like a garden. Any kind of tree can be planted on the dike. In recent years, the trees along the river have not developed well. The entire river is a thousand miles long, and the land is no less than six or seven thousand acres, but there is not a single tree that has grown into timber." (Speaking to this point, the sub-section chief Lu Chuanlun reported that it was because willow branches are used for river defense every year, and the cutting is too excessive.) "Another point, the most important thing today is to order the engineering office to draw a rough map of the entire river, clearly marking the county boundaries on both banks, and each sub-section chief should indicate where there are dangerous sections to facilitate defense planning. These two points are the most important. Everyone must not have the mentality of doing things as before, only caring about the present. Do less things, and be sure to be pragmatic and work hard." "Today, I have sent Li Hou to take over. The section chiefs, secretaries, and sub-section chiefs should provide concise resumes, and a list of engineers and soldiers, and inspect the materials. Each sub-section chief should quickly return to their defense area and watch the river water. Every night from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM, they can report the water situation and other matters to Secretary Chen in Henan, who will forward them to me. If I am not available, they can report to Secretary-General Zhang or Li Yingchang for processing." According to Lu Province's Yellow River defense can be divided into three periods. In the fifth year of Xianfeng, the Yellow River changed its course to the sea, and no one paid attention to defense, allowing it to flow freely. Later, engineers and soldiers were borrowed from Henan for defense, which can be said to be a period of no defense. By the time of the Guangxu period, Governor Zhang Yao began to build dikes on a large scale and diligently sought governance. At that time, with sufficient financial resources and concentrated manpower, the scale was greatly improved in a few years, which can be said to be a period of river engineering reform. During the era of Zhang Huaizhi's supervision of Shandong in the third year of the Republic of China, due to the lack of river affairs talent in the province, some people familiar with river engineering were transferred from Henan to engage in management. Due to sufficient funding, there were many achievements. When Lao Zhichang took office as the director, he hoped for even better governance, so he reorganized the three routes and rebuilt the dikes. However, due to insufficient financial resources, the construction funds could not be received in a certain spring quarter, and the construction work was abandoned, resulting in a breach at Gongjiaba in the lower reaches. After the success of the revolution in the seventeenth year, Fan Qingxu took office as the director and made specific plans for river management, which were quite complete. However, because 1.6 million yuan was needed, Sun Liangcheng dismissed him from his position. After that, the directors were changed several times, and none of them were able to stay in their positions for long, so there were naturally no achievements to speak of. Zhang Lianjia arrived at the bureau on January 6th of the twentieth year, and as of now, it has been five years and three months. With a long time and no shortage of funds, Zhang has also worked hard, so the achievements are quite remarkable. Ten-thirds of the dams have been replaced with stone, and all the river engineers and soldiers have been trained in stages, which can be said to be a period of river engineering on track. Now that Chairman Han is concurrently serving as the director, the administrative power will be used to assist river affairs in the future, and there may not be a risk of a breach this year.

The Xia Lina Steamboat, Traveling Between Siam and Shantou, Runs Aground

The Location is Outside Shantou Port

Fortunately, All Passengers are Safe

Shantou Correspondence: The Shantou-Qianlin shipping line of the Norwegian Dorrison Steamboat Company, which is represented by the Shantou Bonin Company, and in Hong Kong by Qian Tailong, travels regularly between Shantou, Hong Kong, and Qianluo, specializing in carrying passengers and cargo for twelve years. The company has four ships on this route, and the Xia Lina Steamboat is one of them. On the 10th, when the Xia Lina departed from Bangkok, it was loaded with 18,000 bags of rice, 2,000 pieces of general merchandise and timber, and 355 male and female passengers. Due to bad weather along the way, it was delayed until after 4:00 AM on the 19th before arriving outside Shantou Port. It encountered heavy fog and could not see the light of the De Yu Lighthouse, which caused it to run aground. The bow of the ship was stuck in a stone crevice, and the bottom of the stern was damaged and pierced in many places, and water immediately seeped into the rice warehouse. The ship immediately sent a telegram to Shantou Port and other parties for help. In the early morning, the Chao Hai Customs and Bonin Company received the news and immediately notified the Shantou Public Security Bureau and the Cunxin Shantang to provide assistance. De Yu is only ten miles from Shantou by sea, and the voyage can be reached in one hour. The Customs sent the Beidou patrol ship, and the Public Security Bureau also sent patrol boats and inspectors and water police. The Bonin Company rented two electric boats, and the Cunxin Shantang sent a rescue team and many large sailing ships to tow out of the port to provide assistance. At that time, the sun rose in the east, and the fog on the sea dissipated, and the sea was as smooth as a mirror. At 8:00 AM, it sailed to the location where the Xia Lina had an accident and saw the Jiangsu ship, which had returned to Shantou from Siam, stopped there, lowered a sampan, and rescued the Xia Lina passengers to the ship. Because there were many reefs nearby, large ships could not get close. However, it was heard that when the Jiangsu ship and fishing boats rescued passengers, they charged each person four Siamese silver coins to be transported to the Jiangsu ship by fishing boat. It is regrettable that the fishing boats took advantage of the situation. Although the Bonin Company's electric boats and large sailing ships were close to the Xia Lina Steamboat, the seawater had already poured into the second cabin, so they quickly lowered the passengers' luggage and objects in the cabin onto the various sailing ships and transported them to the front of the Customs House, where each person claimed them. The Customs inspectors and police assisted in maintaining order. After this chaotic return, many passengers suffered invisible losses such as picking up the wrong luggage and objects. Fortunately, everyone was safe and was transported in batches until 4:00 PM. As for the rice and general merchandise in the ship, they were also quickly transferred. On the evening of the 19th, more than 2,900 bags of wet rice were recovered. On the 20th, another 6,000 bags were recovered. The tugboat sent from Hong Kong arrived before noon on the 20th. Before noon on the 21st, all the goods were completely recovered. They are now using water pumps to pump out the seawater in the cabin. According to the Bonin Company, they plan to tow it to the Da Jing Ping beach first, repair the hull, and then tow it to the Hong Kong shipyard for repairs. This project will take one or two months at the fastest to complete. The loss of goods this time amounted to more than 100,000 yuan.

The Committee Allocates Funds

To Improve Ping Shui Green Tea

Establish an Improvement Center to Improve Tea Industry Technology

Reach an Agreement with the Zhejiang Construction Department on Cooperation Methods

Hangzhou Correspondence: Chinese tea has always dominated the world. Forty years ago, it was at its peak. The annual export volume of Chinese tea was often more than 2 million dan. In the first year of the Republic of China, it was still 1.48 million dan. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, it fell to 300,000 dan, which was the most depressed period. In recent years, it has gradually increased to 600,000 to 700,000 dan, but it is only one-third of what it was forty years ago. In the world's recent total annual tea trade of 900 million pounds (about 7 million dan), Chinese tea accounts for only 10%. In terms of price, black tea has improved slightly, while green tea has declined. Since foreign tea has flourished, our country's black tea is threatened by India, Ceylon, and Java, and green tea is threatened by Japan. Foreign markets have been plundered, and domestic markets have also been gradually invaded. Foreign black tea sells 20 million pounds in the mainland every year, and the popularity of Taiwan tea in Fujian is even more alarming. If we do not take measures to save it, the future of the tea industry will be unimaginable.

Decline in Production and Sales

Zhejiang is an important tea producing area in China. The most famous teas produced are Ping Shui green tea and Qimen black tea, which are the main players in international trade, and the export volume even exceeds that of Qimen black tea. Longjing, Qiqiang, Liuan, Wuyi, and Pu'er are all treasures of domestic sales, and their shapes, colors, fragrances, and tastes are quite prominent. The total annual tea production in the province is more than 400,000 dan, worth 20 million yuan, accounting for more than one-third of the total export value of Zhejiang's native products. Ping Shui green tea and Wenzhou black tea used to be exported from Shanghai, mostly to the United States, and were very honorable. However, due to the temporary demand exceeding supply and poor commercial organization, tea merchants reduced costs to make profits, and tried to adulterate and color the tea. Everyone followed suit, which led to the deterioration of the quality of Zhejiang tea and the decline in prices. The production volume and sales also decreased as a result. The entire tea industry economy is declining. If we can engage in improvement, improve quality and increase production volume with scientific methods, and transport and sell to existing markets, we will still be able to obtain warm welcome from consumers and have a good chance of revival.

Ping Shui Tea Area

The Ping Shui tea producing area mainly includes seven counties: Shaoxing, Xiaoshan, Shangyu, Zhuji, Shengxian, Xinchang, and Yuyao. The Zhejiang Construction Department should have selected the center of the tea area, the barren land of Haoba Lion Mountain in Shangyu County, which has convenient land and water transportation and good soil quality, in March of last year to establish the Haoba Tea Farm. The mountains there are flat, and the area, including the nearby Embroidery Ball Mountain, is about ten square miles, totaling more than 5,000 acres. 1,000 acres have been cultivated, and more than 300,000 tea seedlings of various types have been planted. A tea industry guidance office has also been established to provide technical guidance to tea farmers in the Ping Shui area. However, due to limited funds, development is difficult. Since Wu Tingsou took over as the Director of the Construction Department, he believed that the development of production and construction must start with improving the province's inherent special products. It was decided to expand and rebuild the original Haoba Lion Mountain newly cultivated tea farm into the Ping Shui Tea Industry Improvement Farm, responsible for handling the improvement of cultivation, manufacturing, and sales matters. However, due to the province's financial difficulties, there was no funding for the start-up. It was requested from the National Economic Committee to subsidize 40,000 yuan in funding in accordance with the Qimen Improvement Farm method. The committee replied by sending Zhao Lianfang, Director of the Agricultural Department, to Zhejiang. The Construction Department sent Zhang Tianyi, Section Chief, and others to accompany him to inspect the Ping Shui tea area. It was believed that it was necessary to improve it in the same way as Qimen. After both parties agreed, they discussed and decided on the method of cooperating with the Zhejiang Province of the Economic Committee to improve green tea and establish a tea industry improvement farm. The start-up cost of 40,000 yuan was to be shared equally by the Economic Committee and the Zhejiang Construction Department. The recurring cost of 12,000 yuan per year was to be allocated from the provincial agricultural and forestry expenses. The Construction Department has already submitted a request to the Economic Committee for funding, so that it can be realized as soon as possible. The main points of the plan to establish a special improvement farm are explored and recorded below:

Improvement Plan

Land Acquisition: This year, it is planned to first acquire 10 acres of construction land, 30 acres of nursery land, and 960 acres of tea land. The price per acre is 10 yuan, totaling 10,000 yuan. The acquisition procedures will be handled by the Shangyu County Government under the order of the Construction Department.

Building Construction: The tea industry improvement farm's buildings are planned to build six offices, including one office and five research offices, as well as ten initial processing workshops, twenty replication workshops, ten warehouses, three cold storage rooms, and staff dormitories.

Purchase of Machinery: This will be carried out in two phases. In the first phase, four tea steaming machines, ten tea frying machines, ten tea kneading machines, and ten tea drying machines will be purchased from Shanghai, as well as two 20-horsepower engines. In the second phase, new-style tea-making machinery will be purchased from Britain and Japan to prepare for expansion.

Improve and Expand Tea Gardens: The original Haoba Lion Mountain newly cultivated tea gardens have mostly not been improved in terms of topography. Roads should continue to be built, drainage ditches should be improved, and the area should be expanded to become a large-scale tea garden.

Conduct Experiments and Improvements: Experiments and improvements are the main purpose of the tea farm. A detailed business plan should be established before the start of each year, and various experiments and research on breeding, cultivation, and manufacturing should be implemented seriously. After the results are available, the promotion department should cooperate with the tea industry guidance offices in various regions to carry out widespread promotion. (April 29th)

Wei Wei, director of the Suzhou Film Studio, happened to be in Wujiang recently performing a new type of drama. Upon hearing this news, he returned to Suzhou on the 29th.

Recent Cultural Developments in the City of Culture

Special Correspondence from Beiping

Last year, a certain higher education authority here said something meaningful: "China no longer has military defense in Beiping, but only cultural defense." At first glance, linking "culture" and "defense" together seems inappropriate, but since the fall of the various passes of the Great Wall in the 22nd year, the signing of the Tanggu Truce Agreement, until last year, after the so-called Meijin-He Yingqin Agreement, in this situation where China is increasing its defenses with freedom and China's garrison is subject to various restrictions, what national defense can China talk about here? Those of us who live here often have the same feeling, which is that if all the cultural institutions in Beiping were removed, then no one would be able to tell whether Beiping belongs to China. Certain country's ronin, Koreans, and even "Manchukuo" officials and "Hebei-East Autonomous Government" officials can walk around the park with their heads held high. Foreign soldiers in red caps are always bumping into each other in the shopping malls. The shops are full of certain country's goods, and advertisements for Lao Du eye drops, University eye drops, etc. are plastered all over the streets and corners. Even the paper used to wrap peanuts in small shops is made of scraps of old Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, Yomiuri Shimbun, or Asahi Shimbun, etc. Under these circumstances, the only thing that can often evoke memories in people's minds and make people aware that they are still within Chinese territory is these cultural institutions and the activities of the people engaged in cultural work. Linking "culture" and "defense" together is ridiculous and sad, but what makes us even more sad is that if we want to find China's national defense here, then apart from this ridiculous and sad so-called "cultural defense," there is really nothing.

The first thing worth mentioning is naturally the activities of the students in various schools. Last year's "December 9th" and "December 16th" demonstrations, as well as the southward expansion propaganda led by the Student Union, added together, made the Beiping student movement to save the country comparable to the Egyptian student anti-British movement, and became the two most meaningful movements in the world last year.
