(28th, Central News Agency dispatch)

粵考察團離梧赴桂林 70

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong inspection delegation left Wuzhou for Guilin at 7:00 AM on the 29th, and will stay overnight before heading to Yongning. (29th, Central News Agency dispatch)

國勞海外部長伊氏談　昨晨拜訪吳市長並應其歡宴　國勞中國分局茶會招待伊氏　在滬視察後將晋京謁我當局 71

Mr. Eastman, Director of the Overseas Department of the International Labour Office (ILO), arrived in Shanghai from Japan a few days ago. Yesterday morning, he visited Mayor Wu and attended his luncheon. The ILO China Branch held a tea party for Mr. Eastman at 5:00 PM at the International Hotel. After 7:00 PM, he attended a banquet hosted by the Pacific International Association. After inspecting various factories and labor conditions in Shanghai, Mr. Eastman will go to Beijing on the 3rd of next month to visit our government authorities, then travel to Beiping before returning to Canada via Japan. Details are as follows:

Visiting the Mayor

Mr. Eastman, Director of the Overseas Department of the ILO, was originally scheduled to attend the Asian Labor Conference in Japan. After the conference was cancelled, Mr. Eastman took the opportunity to come to China from Japan to inspect labor conditions. He arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and stayed at the Cathay Hotel. At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, accompanied by Mr. Cheng Haifeng, Director of the ILO China Branch, Mr. Eastman took a car to the municipal government to visit Mayor Wu. Mayor Wu, along with Secretary Tang Shixuan, received him warmly and led him to visit the construction of Greater Shanghai. Mr. Eastman expressed his admiration for the vigorous construction in this city. He departed at 11:00 AM. At noon, he attended a luncheon hosted by the Mayor at his private residence on Haig Road, accompanied by senior municipal officials.

Welcome Tea Party

Mr. Cheng Haifeng, Director of the ILO China Branch, held a tea party yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM at the ballroom on the 14th floor of the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to welcome Mr. Eastman. Attendees included Mr. and Mrs. Eastman, Cheng Haifeng, Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu, (Representative of Wang Zhinan), Zhao Tiezhang, Lu Jingshi, Zhou Xuexiang, Wang Zhisheng, Lin Kanghou, Zaiboqi, Zhang Kechang, Ye Xianggao, Long Peiyun, Chuan Dewei, Li Mengnan, Yang Youren, Sun Liping, Zhao Shusheng, Canadian Trade Commissioner to China McDonald, and Mrs. Smith. Director Cheng and Section Chief He Tingzhen warmly welcomed the guests and served tea and refreshments. As this was Mr. Eastman's first visit to China, Mr. Cheng introduced and conversed with him individually. The guests and hosts were extremely harmonious. The Pacific International Association hosted a banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Eastman at the International YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road last night at 7:00 PM. The Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions, the Chinese Seamen's Union, the National Postal Workers' Union, and the National Postal Employees' Union, among other industrial and commercial organizations, are also scheduled to jointly host a banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Eastman at the New Asia Restaurant at 7:30 PM this afternoon. The Canadian Trade Commissioner to China will also host a banquet tomorrow.

Remarks by Mr. Eastman

When the reporter met with Mr. Eastman at the International Hotel's ILO Branch tea party yesterday and asked about his future itinerary and the general situation of overseas labor, he said that this was his first visit to China since taking office as Director of the ILO's Overseas Department (the Overseas Department includes the Americas and Asia outside of Europe). He had long heard about the progress of China's material construction and had been eager to visit, but he had few opportunities. This time, he was originally dispatched by the ILO to attend the Asian Labor Conference scheduled to be held this year in Japan. However, he received a notice of cancellation during the trip and took this opportunity to visit your country to inspect labor conditions and make the most enjoyable trip of his life. After arriving here, he was especially grateful for the special hospitality of Director Cheng and the industrial circles. He had visited factories under the guidance of Mr. Cheng the day before and had a very good impression. He hopes to continue to visit other major factories and inspect general labor conditions during his stay here for the next few days. On the 3rd of next month, he will go to Beijing with Mr. Cheng to visit your government authorities. After finishing his business, he will travel north to Beiping, then return to Canada via Japan. Regarding the current situation of overseas labor, the following can be mentioned: Countries that have abolished the gold standard, such as the United Kingdom and Switzerland, have seen improvements in their economic situation, so they have been able to use enterprises to hire more workers and produce and export goods in large quantities. Countries that have adopted the gold standard, such as France, are still in a state of economic panic. In fact, they hire the majority of workers, but the production of goods is limited, with the aim of avoiding overproduction. Therefore, the situation is slightly worse than in the United Kingdom and Switzerland. However, many countries are in a special situation, namely, they can employ a large number of workers as much as possible in the military field, undertaking military work, so the number of unemployed workers is reduced. In the Americas, since Roosevelt became President of the United States, he has been vigorously engaged in reforms of the social system. Unfortunately, the Supreme Court did not approve of Roosevelt's social and economic reform plans, so they could not be fully realized. However, the reforms that have been carried out have fully demonstrated a phenomenon of recovery, and the labor situation has improved slightly. China is a newly emerging industrial country in the world, and the development of its industrial future is immeasurable. In my opinion, China should have legal provisions for the protection of workers at present, so as to avoid the regret of not being able to take measures when industrial development reaches its highest level.

市總工會　籌備慶祝五一　上午九時在寗波同鄉會舉行　全市各廠停工並作播音宜傳 72

The Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions has decided to hold the 50th anniversary of the International Labor Day on May 1st (tomorrow) at 9:00 AM in the auditorium of the Ningbo Native Place Association, and has requested major newspapers to publish special issues. Members of the Municipal Party Committee, Lu Jingshi, and others will be responsible for broadcasting speeches. Details are as follows:

Notice of Participation

The Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions notified all trade unions in the city: "Regarding the notice, the 1st of May is the International Labor Day. Our federation will hold a commemorative meeting at 9:00 AM on the morning of that day at the Ningbo Native Place Association on Xizang Road. We hereby notify you to send ten representatives to attend the meeting and participate in the grand event. Please do not delay. We hereby notify you."

Citywide Shutdown

"May 1st" is International Labor Day. In order to express their warm celebration, all trade unions in the city have decided to follow the factory law promulgated by the central government and have workers stop work for one day on that day. In addition to the trade unions directly notifying all workers to stop work, they have also sent letters to the factories informing them to pay wages as usual. The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions has already decided to transfer all the wages for the May 1st commemorative worker shutdown to purchase machines for birthday celebrations, and has submitted a request to the municipal government to order all manufacturers to deduct the amount on their behalf.

Broadcast Propaganda

In addition to preparing to hold a commemorative meeting, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions has also requested Shenbao, Xinwen, Mingbao, Dagongbao, Shishi, Zhonghua, and other newspapers to issue special issues. In addition, Lu Jingshi, Zhou Xuexiang, Zhang Kechang, Lu Muqin, Long Peiyun, and others will be responsible for broadcasting speeches.

律師公會電請　增國民大會代表名額 75

Shanghai Lawyers Association members Zhang Shijie, Yang Li, Yan Yinwu and others have suggested to consider increasing the number of representatives to the National Assembly. The association sent a telegram to the Legislative Yuan yesterday, which reads: "To Sun, President of the Nanjing Legislative Yuan, and all members, upon reading the Shenbao of April 25, regarding the number of representatives of free professional groups to the National Assembly, the Standing Committee decided to be 58, of which the number of representatives of lawyers groups was considered too high by Committee Member Dai Chuanxian, and it was suggested to reduce it. Lawyers are widespread throughout the country, numbering tens of thousands, and their position in society and the country is also very important. Moreover, the main task of the Central Government in convening the National Assembly is to formulate a constitution and exercise the powers conferred by the constitution. If representatives of lawyers groups attend with a considerable number of representatives, they will contribute more to the constitutional cause, and it will also be beneficial to the vigorous implementation of the rule of law. The number of representatives should be appropriately increased in accordance with the central allocation principle, which is more appropriate. We hereby telegraph to your esteemed Yuan, and when deliberating on the number of representatives of the lawyers groups to the National Assembly, please make an appropriate increase. The future of the rule of law is very fortunate. Shanghai Lawyers Association."

The Shanghai Times News reported that the special zone telephone problem committee and the telephone company have reached a stalemate regarding the issue of user fees. Many users in various districts have been inquiring about payment methods to the committee in recent days. The committee has replied to them separately, as follows: The Fourth Branch of the Second Special District Citizens' Union sent a letter to the Special Zone Telephone Problem Committee, and the committee replied: "Regarding the letter, refusing to pay telephone fees is a passive countermeasure to the telephone company's decision to charge fees. We should insist to the end, and this determination will not change until the goal of canceling the new rules is achieved. In addition to our committee ignoring the company's final notice and cutting off the telephone line today to show our responsibility, we hereby reply and ask you to inform us." The committee also replied to Taixiang Yanhao and Jianguang Guiyuanhao: "Regarding the letter, refusing to pay telephone fees is a passive countermeasure to the telephone company's decision to charge fees by the number of calls. We should insist to the end, and this determination will not change until the goal of canceling the new rules is achieved. Your firm's ability to lead by example, take care of the interests of all users, and support our committee's struggle with its spirit of unity and strength of determination is admirable. Other users are inspired and will surely follow suit. Once there are too many disconnections, the telephone company will inevitably panic. The ultimate victory depends on the unity of purpose of the majority of our users. We hereby reply and ask you to take note."

Municipal Government Convened Various Groups Yesterday to Discuss Unified Implementation of Party and National Flags, Decided to Organize a Committee to Handle It 86

The Municipal Government of this city convened representatives from various agencies and organizations in this city at 1:00 PM yesterday to discuss the Shanghai Municipality Party and National Flag unified implementation method. It was decided to organize an implementation committee and pass the committee organizational regulations. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives: Those attending yesterday included Wu Huanru from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Yuan Hongjun from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Xu Zhenzhi from the Health Bureau, Yao Changqi from the Education Bureau, Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association, Zhang Yichen and Liu Zhongying from the First Special District Citizens' Federation, Huang E from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Huang Zaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association, Li Dachao from the Municipal Government, Wang Manyun from the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession, Li Dachao from the Aviation Association (concurrently), and Zhang Zilian, Chi Jianxian, and Guo Zhongyi from the Party and National Flag Production and Sales Headquarters. Li Dachao presided over the meeting.

Resolutions:

Following ceremonial procedures, Chairman Li Dachao first reported on the convocation of various agencies and organizations to discuss the Party and National Flag method, and then began discussing and resolving the following items: Passed the Shanghai Party and National Flag Unified Implementation Committee Regulations; The attending groups nominated the Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Government, China Aviation Association, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession, First Special District Citizens' Federation, Education Bureau, etc., as standing committee members, and the Municipal Government and Municipal Party Headquarters will convene standing committee meetings regularly; Propaganda and promotion should be conducted for three months, until National Day; The propaganda outline will be initiated by the Municipal Party Headquarters and then passed by the standing committee meeting.

Committee Regulations:

Shanghai Party and National Flag Unified Implementation Committee Regulations: The name of this committee is the Shanghai Party and National Flag Unified Implementation Committee, which is organized by the Municipal Government and Municipal Party Headquarters convening various agencies and organizations. The purpose of this committee is to promote the meaning of the Party and National Flag and to universally promote the unification of the Party and National Flag in order to promote the national spirit. This committee will have a committee, composed of the following agencies and organizations: Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Government, Garrison Headquarters, Public Security Bureau, Social Affairs Bureau, Education Bureau, Health Bureau, Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession, French Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, General Labor Union, Education Association, Farmers' Association, Citizens' Federation, China Aviation Association Collection Team Headquarters, Party and National Flag Production and Sales Headquarters. This committee will have seven standing committee members, mutually elected by the above-mentioned agencies and organizations. This committee will hold regular meetings once a month. Extraordinary meetings may be convened when necessary. The staff members required by this committee will be transferred or hired from various agencies and organizations. This committee should undertake the following matters: (A) Propaganda matters concerning the meaning of the Party and National Flag; (B) Party and National Flag unified implementation matters; (C) Organizing Party and National Flag reviews in stages and districts. The committee members and standing committee members of this committee are all honorary positions. The necessary expenses for this committee will be raised separately. The committee's office will be temporarily located in the office of the China Aviation Construction Association. These regulations will be implemented upon resolution and passage by this meeting. Amendments may be made by this committee if there are any incomplete details.

Tofu Industry Association Held General Meeting Yesterday 88

Tofu is one of the main staple foods, rich in nutrients. Those engaged in this business in this city are scattered everywhere, totaling as many as 308. However, there has been no organization until last year when the Shanghai Tofu Industry Association was established to promote unity. Yesterday afternoon, the association held its second membership general meeting at the Qiaojiazha office in the South City. Attendees included Huang Tieren from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhu Zhongqing from the Social Affairs Bureau, Sun Mingqi from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the general meeting presidium Tan Yueming, Gu Qi, Qiao Guifang, and 206 members from the city, including Shi Yizheng and Shen Xianlu. They discussed industry regulations and set prices, creating a lively atmosphere, it was said.

Economic Situation of Tongren Hospital 89

Tongren Hospital in this city published its 1935 report, stating that the 727,000 yuan in donations accumulated by the hospital over 20 years was intended to be used to build a new hospital, school, and laboratory building. The funds were either deposited in the Mei Feng Bank and Puyi Silver Company or loaned to Puyi Real Estate Company. The collapse of the Mei Feng Bank caused a major blow to the hospital's finances. The planned building will be postponed indefinitely. At most, it is hoped that 60% of the deposited funds can be recovered, and most of that will come from Puyi Real Estate Company. Due to poor market conditions last year and the large influx of refugees from disaster areas into Shanghai, the hospital suffered a deficit of 6,000 yuan at the end of the year. Most of these refugees who came to the hospital were unable to pay, and because their fields and houses were flooded, they had nowhere to go. Sometimes the hospital even provided them with small amounts of money to help them get on their feet in Shanghai. Last year, a total of 16,335 yuan in donations was received, and 29,698 yuan in assistance was provided by the Municipal Council and American churches. There were a total of 113,300 outpatient visits and 3,000 inpatients. It is hoped that enthusiastic philanthropists will continue to generously provide assistance so that the hospital's expenses can be balanced.

Page 13

Yangtze River Shipping Experiencing Unprecedented Decline, Less Than Two-Fifths of What It Was Four Years Ago; Only Japanese Ships' Business Holds the Top Position 93

The Yangtze River is the richest area for Chinese native products, and is the central region for the production of various grains. From Shanghai to Hankou, the purchasing power of the four provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei is the strongest, especially for imported goods, with salt and sugar being the main food products. Therefore, foreign ships operating on this route are doing everything they can to compete for business. Since the January 28th Incident, each year has been worse than the last, and the volume of goods shipped has

Plummeted

Compared to four years ago, it is less than two-fifths. The main reason for this year's sharp decline in shipping is the depletion of social finances. The purchasing power of the people along the river has been greatly reduced. In previous years, those handling goods could obtain financing from banks and money shops, and the recipients of the goods could pay after selling them. Therefore, the flow of goods was not hindered. This year, the banking industry has restricted lending, and all goods must be

Transacted in Cash

This has bound those handling goods with financial restrictions, making procurement and transportation impossible. This is the biggest reason for the sharp decline in Yangtze River shipping. The six Yangtze River shipping companies have been continuously losing money for three years. Last year, they changed their approach and formed an alliance to share profits and losses. Although freight rates have been increased and commissions reduced, the volume of goods coming and going is less than in previous years. Even with the alliance, they are still losing money. Now, the six companies are planning to

Increase Freight Rates, Including a One-Tenth Increase in Shallow Water Freight Rates, to Make Up for the Losses. However, the volume of packaged goods has already been fundamentally taken away by Yangzi Company ships that do not participate in the profit-sharing alliance, as well as the diversion of cargo to postal packages, sailing ships, and trains. As a result, there is even less cargo being transported to the Yangtze River from this area. Starting in April, the Yangtze River ships of a certain large company among the six companies are sometimes only carrying one-tenth to two-tenths of their capacity on each voyage. Even the best ones are only carrying four-tenths to five-tenths of their cargo. When reporters inquired with various customs brokers on this route, it was claimed that Yangtze River customs brokers have always paid customs duties on behalf of customers three times a year. Now, the new regulations of the customs require

Monthly Tax Payments, Which many customs brokers cannot afford to pay, so they have to reduce their business. This is also one of the reasons for the decrease in Yangtze River freight. Furthermore, the volume of domestic sugar being transported to the Yangtze River has always been large, but now, due to the sharp drop in the price of smuggled sugar, the sales of domestic sugar on the Yangtze River have been invisibly affected. Normally, during the flood season, the business of Yangtze River ships is supposed to improve, but this year is different. If there is no turnaround in April of the lunar calendar, then there is no hope for the Yangtze River ships' business in the latter half of this year. As for goods coming downstream, since rice has been banned from being exported from Jiujiang, Wuhu, Changsha, and other ports, there is no longer any transportation of miscellaneous grains downstream. Only

Japanese Ships on the Yangtze River, Because They Have a Large Volume of Transit Cargo Coming and Going, Have Been Occupying the Top Position in the Entire Yangtze River Shipping Business, Regardless of Whether They Participate in the Profit-Sharing Alliance. The Changsha route in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River is slightly better, while the section between Hankou and Yichang is even more superior due to the large volume of goods being transferred to ships going to Sichuan. Shanghai direct ships to Chongqing experienced a surge in cargo due to President Chiang's recent decision to go to Sichuan. The Fuyang ship of the Sanbei Company, which departed on the 2nd, was already fully loaded yesterday. Those who registered to ship cargo later even had no space available.

Continuous Rain in This City for Several Days; Rain Stopped Last Night, Hope for Sunny Weather; Strong Winds and High Tides Outside Wusongkou 95

This city has been experiencing continuous rain in recent days, and the weather is turning cold. The wind is also strong outside Wusongkou, resulting in high tides for several days. The details are as follows:

Rain Stopped Last Night: This city experienced a sudden onset of wind on the 26th, and the following day, wind and rain came together, continuing until last night, when the rain finally stopped. At the same time, the air pressure has returned to high. Although the sky has not yet cleared by nightfall, there is hope for sunny weather, and the climate is also expected to warm up. However, prices for commodities such as rice, grains, and vegetables have remained firm due to the impact of the continuous rain.

High Tides at Wusongkou: Due to strong winds, the tides outside Wusongkou have been quite high in recent days. According to records from the Dredging Bureau, the water level outside Wusongkou reached 12 feet 3.8 inches on the 26th, 11 feet 4 inches on the 27th, and 12 feet 2 inches on the 28th. Guo Yuequan, Wang Ruling, and Yang Zhaoqing, Chinese detectives from the Narcotics Division of the Public Concession Police, learned that Yang Yonglin, a native of Shaoxing, was secretly selling the drug red pills for profit inside No. 83 Yangshupu Road. The scale was grand, with 66 bags of manufactured drug pills, totaling 120,000 pills, and several bags of unfinished pills, 40 taels of heroin, and a large quantity of white powder materials. One Chinese man and one Chinese woman were arrested, along with equipment such as machines and coal boxes, and taken to the Public Security Bureau. Yuanshang Outailang, Yang, and Chen, the two drug dealers, were taken back to the police station. Outailang was sent to the Japanese consulate for questioning. Yesterday morning, Yang Yonglin and Chen Sanda were handed over to Criminal Court 3 of the First Special District Court. He requested that the court issue an official letter to transfer them to the Shanghai District Court. The case was postponed for further investigation, it was said. Following the report of the Chinese and Western detectives clarifying the process of solving the case and questioning the two defendants, their statements were evasive. However, if he put a white paper, Tan's two sons might face unfavorable consequences in the future. The ransom demanded was twenty thousand yuan. Tan reported the letter to the Gordon Road Police Station, which ordered him to comply and secretly dispatched detectives to Tan's vicinity to monitor the situation. The following day, Tan received a second letter stating that the red paper had been seen. Now that he was willing to pay, he was asked to provide five hundred yuan for travel expenses to be sent to the Xinzha Bridge. Currently, the case is requested to be postponed because the home of Zhu Chengde, located at 156, Lane 617, Xiaoshadu Road, was robbed on February 24th of this year. It was found that Zhu and Tan lived in the same lane. Afterwards, Zhu Chengde suddenly received a letter from the robbers stating that they had intended to rob the home of Tan Magen but had mistakenly robbed his residence, for which they were deeply sorry. Therefore, the police need to investigate this point. Furthermore, according to Tan Lixing's testimony, the defendant Wang Asi confessed that he was a beggar. Sun Yin Abuses Maid to Death, Forensic Examination Completed, Prosecutor Files Indictment, Trial Result Awaits Investigation 101

Sun Yin, a local woman, lived at 43 Shagang, Gaoqiao, Pudong. In August of last year, she bought a six-year-old girl named Donglan as a maid through an intermediary. Because the girl was young and somewhat clumsy, Sun Yin felt that she was disobedient and often beat her. On December 30th, Donglan somehow fell and injured her head, resulting in her death. Neighbors, feeling indignant, falsely used the name Huang Zhiqiang and reported the incident to the local police station, requesting a thorough investigation into the abuse leading to death. Upon receiving the order, the police station detained Sun Yin and sent her to the District Court. Prosecutor Li Xulin, along with examiners, went to the countryside to exhume and examine the body, but the true cause of death was unclear. Therefore, Donglan's body was sent to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for autopsy. It is now learned that the Forensic Institute has completed the autopsy, and its examination report has been sent to the court. Prosecutor Li has filed a public indictment against Sun Yin in accordance with the law. The indictment states that Sun Yin bought Donglan to be her maid, and reviewing the original case file sent by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, it has been verified that this is the case. Therefore, Sun Yin's claim that she adopted Donglan to be a daughter and companion, and not a maid, is not credible. Her actions constitute a violation of Article 296, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. The part concerning the death will be dealt with separately. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Judge Cai Dingcheng of the Criminal Division of the Third Court presided over the trial. The defendant Sun Yin hired lawyers Jin Yu and Fang Gang to defend her. Sun Yin testified that she was 45 years old and adopted Donglan, a six-year-old girl from Shalang, last year as a foster daughter, not a maid. Huang Jincai, the local bailiff, testified that Donglan was indeed Sun Yin's foster daughter. Lawyer Jin then requested the court to investigate the household registration office of the local police station to determine whether the deceased Donglan was his foster daughter or a maid. Judge Cai reviewed the testimony and ordered the case to be postponed for further investigation. The defendant remained on bail.

Wu Lusheng, a local resident, 47 years old, solely owned Wu Zhenxing Hardware Store at 491 Mei Bai Ge Road and Zhenxing Hardware Store at 621 Henan Road. Judge Chuan Lin reviewed the testimony and ordered a postponement for further interrogation. Wu Tang was released on a bail of 5,000 yuan from the store. Cao was remanded in custody.

Yonghetang Accused of Containing Toxic Substances, Shi Yuanlong Found Not Guilty Yesterday, Violation Part Sent to the Violation Court 103

Yonghetang Pharmacy, located at 23 Shunqing Lane, Lane 7, Shanxi Road, was opened by Shi Zhenghua from Shaoxing. Shi passed away due to illness on June 12, 1934, and the pharmacy was then managed by his eldest son, Shi Yuanlong (also known as Wenlong). Two types of phlegm-relieving and cough-suppressing drugs produced by the pharmacy, "Kumquat Frost" and "Pinellia Ferment," had a wide sales network, especially inland. The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau tested these two drugs and found that they contained toxic substances such as morphine, codeine, and noscapine. The bureau sent a letter to the First Special District Court to investigate. The Special Court issued an order to the General Police Station. Chinese Detective Su Changsheng and Detective Ni Jiaxin purchased the aforementioned drugs from the pharmacy. Then the Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang filed a public prosecution according to Article 257 of the Criminal Law. Under the interrogation of the First Special Court, Shi Yuanlong paid 1,000 yuan in bail to wait for the drug test results for further verification. During the postponement period, the First Special Court received official documents from Jiangxi and Zhejiang provinces, stating that the above-mentioned two drugs contained toxic substances. The First Special Court sent the remaining doses of the two drugs tested by the Shanghai Municipal Health Testing Institute on January 11 and March 13, 1932, as well as those purchased by the police this time, to the Forensic Institute of the Ministry of Administration of the same court for testing. The institute has now reported the testing results to the court. Therefore, yesterday morning, Judge Qian Hongye opened the First Criminal Court to continue the trial. The report of the Forensic Institute was announced in court, stating that the drug tested on January 11, 1932, contained opium, and the drug tested on March 13 contained suspected noscapine. The drugs purchased by the police could not be proven to contain toxic substances. The police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that according to the testing results, the defendant should not be guilty. Please let the court to decide freely. However, there is no doubt that the defendant violated the regulations on prepared drugs. The defendant submitted two photos of certificates from the Health Testing Institute proving that his drugs did not contain toxins, but he could not produce the originals, which showed that he had the suspicion of destroying evidence. The police should investigate and prosecute him in another case. After the defendant's lawyer defended Shi, Judge Qian declared in court that Shi Yuanlong was not guilty, and the violation part was sent to the violation court for trial.

Using the Name of Imparting Culture, Tan Tian Commits Fraud and Obtains Money, Wang Yu Yuan, Manager of Hankou Da Shu Book Company, Files Prosecution, Defendant on the Run, Waiting for Arrest and Trial 107

Tan Tian, a bookseller from Anhui, raised funds in October of the year before last to open a book and newspaper cooperative in Wangping Street, publishing various books. Recently, Wang Yu Yuan, the manager of Da Shu Book Company on Jiaotong Road in Hankou, who is from Shaoxing, commissioned a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the Second Special Court's Criminal Division against Tan Tian for pre-selling books with the intention of fraud, requesting legal action and including a civil suit, requesting a judgment to return the book payment of 1,584 yuan and 6 jiao. The essence of the self-suit states that the defendant Tan Tian opened a book and newspaper cooperative, compiling and printing books such as Twenty-Six Histories, Dietary Goods of Past Dynasties, Foreign Official Chronicles, New Yuan History, Qing History Biographies, etc., publishing advertisements in newspapers and issuing pre-sale book coupons. The self-litigant was entrusted to sell on commission, and successively set the price for Sixty-Six copies of the Twenty-Six Histories, Twenty-Seven copies of the New Yuan History, Twenty-Five copies of the Qing History Biographies, and one copy each of Dietary Goods of Past Dynasties, totaling 1,584 yuan and 6 jiao in book money. Between the winter of 1934 and January and February of the following year, the book payment was remitted to Tan Tian in succession, with receipt as proof. According to the pre-sale catalog of the cooperative, the Twenty-Six Histories would first publish five types, such as the Records of the Grand Historian, the History of the Han, and the History of the Jin. The remaining fifteen types, such as the Five Dynasties, Liao, Jin, Song History New Compilation, Yuan History New Compilation, and Twenty-Six History Research, would be published and delivered to the subscribers by the end of 1935. However, Tan Tian received the book payment but failed to publish the pre-sold books by the due date, nor did he return the book payment. Using delaying tactics until about October of last year, the cooperative closed down. In order to shirk responsibility, a temporary communication office was set up at 8 Songshan Road. The self-litigant was urged by customers who had pre-ordered the books and found it difficult to cope. However, the defendant Tan Tian, in the name of imparting culture, engaged in fraudulent means, which constituted the crime of fraud under Article 339 of the Criminal Code. The court is requested to detain him for punishment and order him to return the full amount of book money paid by the self-litigant. Upon receiving the petition, Judge Qiu Huanying went to the Second Criminal Division at 9:00 AM yesterday to summon the defendant. Only Xi Xiangguan, the agent lawyer of the self-litigant Wang Yu Yuan, appeared in court. After explaining the case, Judge Qiu said that it was impossible to summon the defendant Tan Tian, so he ordered that the case be tried again after the defendant was arrested.

Dismissed Chinese Detective He Qingen Sentenced for Theft, Sentenced to Seven Years and Seven Months in Prison 110

He Qingen, a Chinese detective from Beiping, who was formerly a Chinese detective in the Special Agency of the General Police Station, was arrested by the police and sent to the First Special Court on suspicion of using weapons to kidnap people for ransom after being dismissed. He was sentenced to seven years in prison. Later, he was given a reduced sentence due to a general amnesty, and he was released from prison in August of last year. Recently, He's father was found to be hiding firearms, and Chinese Detective Feng Baishun, Detective Wang Yongjun, Sun Wenxi and others from the Chengdu Road Police Station brought He Qingen, and his accomplices Tao Shiying, Shen Xiangen and the three of them, along with two pistols and fifteen bullets, into the police station. It was found that He et al. had committed armed gang theft in the concession. They were sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and the trial was concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Tan Xin announced the verdict in court. He Qingen was sentenced to seven years and seven months in prison and deprived of his civil rights for eight years. Tao Shiying was sentenced to five years and six months in prison, and Shen Gengen was sentenced to three years and three months in prison. The seized guns and ammunition were confiscated.

Traffic Bank Republic of China Year 24 Business Report 118

Introduction

It has been a year since the last general meeting of shareholders. I still remember that the last business report briefly mentioned the bank's efforts to improve and plan for economic recovery. Now, as time passes, reviewing the work achievements and reforms implemented in the past year, we have been gradually advancing according to the established direction. However, due to the difficult times, we have not been able to fully achieve our expectations. In this year, international financial policies have become more turbulent, and changes in the domestic financial system have become a record in China's economic history. At this time, the bank realizes the importance of its mission and can only strive to adjust finance and develop industries, hoping to contribute to the cause and live up to the expectations of the government and society. All measures are based on the original intention of striving for stability, so as not to lose prudence in the midst of courageous progress. This is something that can be gratifying to our shareholders. Now, a summary of the domestic and international economic situation, a brief description of the bank's business development, and the direction of future efforts are listed for your consideration.

1. Overview of Domestic and International Economy

In recent years, the domestic economy has remained depressed, and financial business has remained difficult to develop. All these facts show that we cannot satisfy our long-held expectations. Even if we look at the foreign economy, the special development of military industries and the increase in economic indexes, the currency competition between gold standard and non-gold standard countries is as antagonistic as in the previous year. The continued concentration of world gold and silver in the United States has become even more pronounced. Therefore, the economic policies of various countries almost all focus on the improvement of the monetary system. China has also taken the relief of industry and commerce and the implementation of legal tender as the central work of the whole year. Let's discuss it separately.

A. International Economy

In the past year, the international economic situation has shown slight improvement. Indexes such as production, consumption, and prices in various countries have increased, but the progress of international trade is still slow. Methods such as controlling industries and raising tariffs continue to be implemented, and currency wars are becoming more and more intense. Looking at the international situation, it is likely to move towards managed currency and stable currency values. First, let's talk about the United States.

Last year, the United States passed the Silver Purchase Act, stipulating that gold and silver reserves must meet a ratio of three to one, or raise the silver price to the coinage parity of one dollar and twenty-nine cents per ounce. This year, this plan is still in progress. The price of silver continues to rise from five corners four minutes eight seven five. In April, the US government decided to raise the price of silver twice within a month, first to seven corners one minute and then to seven corners seven minutes five seven. With speculators taking the opportunity to buy, it rose to a peak of eight corners one minute. Silver flowed out of various countries, leading Italy and Mexico to ban silver exports, and Mexico even declared silver nationalized. The gold standard group also had difficulty maintaining its position. In view of this situation, the US government had to slightly ease the situation, even though it still had to purchase 140 million yuan of silver according to its plan. In May, it ordered the ban on the import of foreign silver coins and changed its silver purchase method. The price of silver began to decline and finally saw a low price of four corners nine minutes seven five at the end of the year. In total, the United States purchased 543.8 million ounces of silver within a year, nearly doubling the amount of the previous year.

The silver purchase situation in the United States is as described above. As for the United Kingdom in the gold pound group, it still follows the policy adopted when it abandoned the gold standard in 1931 and continues to depreciate the currency. At the end of the year, the exchange rate of the gold pound against the French franc has fallen by more than 40%.

As for other European countries that maintained the gold standard, they generally encountered extremely serious financial panic during the year and adopted currency tightening policies one after another. However, due to the depressed domestic economy and sluggish export trade, although they restricted the import of foreign goods in many ways, funds still inevitably flowed out. In addition, at the beginning of the year, a coup occurred in France, and the situation in Italy and Austria became increasingly tense. The European situation became more and more unstable, and funds from France, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Switzerland fled. In March, Belgium had to reduce the parity of the Belgian currency by 28% to save it. The Dutch currency was even more shaken. Affected by this, the French franc was also difficult to maintain. Although the interest rate was raised again and again, it still had no effect. Fortunately, with the unified assistance of the United Kingdom, the United States, and the Bank for International Settlements, it returned to calm. However, in March, April, May and June, its gold reserves decreased by 11,618,000,000 French francs. The serious situation can be generally seen.

The prosperity of the international community is tied to the development of its trade, and a stable exchange rate is the only way to develop international trade. The financial turmoil in various countries is extremely detrimental to economic recovery. Therefore, in May of this year, the US State Department declared that the stability of international currency is an important part of the US foreign trade plan. At the same time, its Congress had a proposal to authorize the President to convene an international conference. The International Chamber of Commerce held in Paris in June also passed a resolution advising countries to strive for international exchange rate stability. In July, the American banker Morgan went to London again and met with the British Prime Minister to jointly stabilize the exchange rate. If all these plans can be realized, it will not only be the key to the world's prosperity, but also the benefit of China's economy.

B. Domestic Economy

In the first half of the year, the domestic economy was still affected by the US silver purchase, and the loss of floods in various places exacerbated the economic panic. Production sharply decreased, prices fell miserably, and agricultural exports also declined. The outflow of silver was still difficult to stop, and the contraction of currency and the shortage of tax revenue not only made industry and commerce increasingly depressed, but also made the silver and money industry feel difficult to cope with.

The government, in view of this, deeply knows that the remedy cannot be delayed. In February, it promulgated measures to encourage the re-import of silver, and in April, it signed an agreement with foreign banks to stop the export of silver. The situation was eased. Unexpectedly, in early April, two Shanghai foreign exchange trading houses successively closed down, and the market situation suddenly felt tense. The turnover of the money industry fell into exhaustion again. With the relief of the Traffic Bank, the Central Bank, and the Bank of China, it was barely maintained. By May, deposit withdrawals occurred in Qingdao and other places. Many silver and money industries in Shanghai, Tianjin, Ningbo, and Guangzhou also suspended business and reorganized. The government allocated 25 million yuan of financial bonds, which were received by the Money Industry Supervision Committee and reorganized into a syndicate loan committee to handle loans. In addition, 20 million yuan of national treasury securities were allocated to establish an industry and commerce loan committee to implement relief separately. The crisis was safely passed. After the end of May, the market situation was still slightly loosened, and the "Hua Tou Jia Shui" (premium for silver dollars) always hovered at the highest peak of seven corners. All parties, in view of the difficult situation, deeply knew that the improvement of the credit system could not be delayed, and that stabilizing hearts and minds would be impossible without flattening the Hua Tou Jia Shui. Therefore, the Traffic Bank and the Bank of China expressed their willingness to adjust as much as possible for the banks and trading houses that needed Hua Tou. The silver and money industries association agreed that the Traffic Bank and the Bank of China would be the central exchange for foreign exchange instruments. Therefore, trading houses lacking silver dollars could borrow Hua Tou from the national treasury with collateral, and the Hua Tou Jia Shui gradually eased. At the same time, the Chamber of Commerce and the banking industry also promoted the acceptance of bills of exchange, and the market situation gradually became active.

The above-mentioned measures are still a temporary solution. On November 3, the government promulgated emergency decrees to reform the currency system, stipulating that the banknotes issued by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Traffic Bank are legal tender, and established a Currency Issuance Reserve Management Committee to unify issuance and centralize reserves. All holders of silver coins and silver should exchange them for legal tender. The central banks, the Bank of China, and the Traffic Bank conducted unlimited trading of foreign exchange, which went smoothly. Many foreign banks in Shanghai also expressed their willingness to cooperate. The Currency Issuance Reserve Management Committee was established on November 5. All issuance reserves of banks that have stopped issuing banknotes, as well as banknotes that have been printed but not issued, and those that have been issued and recovered, were designated to be received separately by the Traffic Bank, the Central Bank, and the Bank of China, and to exchange local silver.

This new monetary system is the beginning of the government's overall plan to improve finance and economy. The first effect is to stabilize the external exchange rate. Then, prices will gradually rise. The foreign exchange market price has not changed at all until the end of the year. In terms of prices, Shanghai wholesale prices in December increased by 13.4% compared to September, export prices increased by 19.4%, and import prices increased by 17.2%. The impact of this price increase on import and export trade can be seen from the import and export trade balance in the three months of winter. In October, the trade deficit was 12,776,023 yuan. In November, it decreased to 12,203,141 yuan. However, some of the goods were ordered before November. In December, it turned into a trade surplus of 5,351,427 yuan. From then on, efforts to improve the domestic economy may continue to improve.

Looking at the domestic and international economic situation as a whole, it is complicated and intricate, and it is not limited to the above. The stability of the international exchange market and the balance of world trade are the key elements for the recovery of the world economy. The foundation for the recovery of prosperity in China's economic circles and the development of various businesses in the banking industry will also be seen from this.

2. Business Situation

The bank is a bank for developing national industries. In terms of its mission, it has the responsibility to maintain and regulate various industries. In terms of the entire financial system, it also takes mutual assistance and cooperation as the principle with its peers. The seriousness of the domestic economic situation in the past year has been described above. The financial industries are in urgent need of relief and support. The expectations of the bank are also increasing. It is difficult to cope with the difficulties and heavy responsibilities. Therefore, on the one hand, it absorbs idle funds to strengthen its strength, and on the other hand, it chooses the urgent matters and carries out operations in different ways. Although it feels difficult to achieve, there are still visible results. Now, the business situation of this year is described separately.

(1) Deposits: The total balance of the bank's deposits in the 24th year of the Republic of China was over 33,147,400 yuan, an increase of over 89,427,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 118,482,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of fixed deposits was over 76,200,000 yuan, an increase of over 10,900,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 23,065,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of current deposits was over 244,030,000 yuan, an increase of over 72,744,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 85,425,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of bank drafts and miscellaneous deposits was over 11,244,000 yuan, an increase of over 5,781,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 9,991,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. According to the bank's historical deposits, they have always increased without decreasing. The increase in this year is even greater. The reason is that the market is depressed, and there are many financial accidents, so deposits have a natural trend of concentration. However, it is also due to the bank's efforts to serve the society. The analysis of the increase in various deposits shows that current deposits are still the most, followed by fixed deposits, and bank drafts and miscellaneous deposits are the least. Among the current deposits, those that can be paid and received with passbooks have increased the most. The increase in fixed deposits shows a good phenomenon of the development of public savings. Analyzing and comparing the figures in each district, the increase in the Shanghai district accounts for nearly two-thirds of the total. Other districts such as Zhejiang, Hong Kong, Xiamen, Hankou, and Zhengzhou also have excellent results. However, the two districts of Northeast Changchun and Shenyang failed to make as much progress as possible due to the complex local currency system and financial situation. The Tianjin district also failed to make as much progress as possible due to environmental reasons. Otherwise, the overall increase would be more than this.

(2) Remittances: The total amount of remittances from the bank in the 24th year was over 457,049,000 yuan, an increase of over 166,007,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 246,425,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The total amount of purchased drafts was over 293,318,000 yuan, an increase of over 115,641,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 187,098,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. This is a significant improvement. The bank has always paid attention to communicating remittances to assist the flow of industrial and American finance. This year, branches have continued to add remittance locations, expand distribution, and strive for simple procedures and convenience for customers. Since the currency system changed, remittances from various places have been uniformly exempted from water and transfer, and the turnover has become more flexible, resulting in the expected results.

The only districts where remittances and purchased drafts decreased this year were Changchun and Zhejiang. The reason is that the Changchun district was affected by the local management of remittances and the transfer of funds, and the Zhejiang district was due to the turmoil in the money industry in Ningbo, which led to a reduction in the outflow of funds. However, the total number of reductions in the two districts is not as much as one-tenth of the increase in the Shanghai district. Other districts such as Hong Kong, Xiamen, Tianjin, Jinan, Hankou, and Zhengzhou also have a large increase, which shows a glimpse of the remittance business in this year.

(3) Loans and Investments: The total balance of the bank's loans and investments in the 24th year was over 254,678,000 yuan, an increase of over 39,786,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 75,578,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of fixed loans was over 63,695,000 yuan, which is the same as the previous two years. The balance of current loans was over 150,288,000 yuan, which is an increase of over 29,329,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 52,471,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of discounted loans was over 5,942,000 yuan, which is the same as the 23rd year and an increase of over 3,524,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The balance of valuable securities was over 34,751,000 yuan, an increase of over 11,380,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 8,600,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. Excluding valuable securities, the total balance of the three loans, fixed-term, current-term and discounted, this year was over 219,925,000 yuan, compared with the total balance of 191,520,000 yuan in the 23rd year, an increase of 28,400,000 yuan. Analyzing its increased content, commodity and factory mortgage loans are still the most, followed by security mortgage loans, and then by loans to institutions and groups. The bank has always emphasized credit on goods in its loan methods. In addition to adding warehouses and directly doing commodity mortgages, it also pays attention to industrial and agricultural loans. Therefore, the number of commodity mortgage loans has increased the most, and factory mortgage loans have also achieved success. The following is a list of the investment amounts of various commodity mortgages, mortgage financing and investments this year.

From the above observation, the investment in various commodities this year is not only considerable in amount, but also evenly distributed. In the future, if the environment permits, it will continue to seek development in this area. The reason why the security mortgage loan has increased more is that the government has actively carried out various construction projects this year and issued public bonds, which were borne and mortgaged by the bank more. In order to maintain national credit and assist colleagues in regulating the market, bond mortgage arbitrage has also been done. The bank, with its position and mission, has made inevitable investments. In addition, since the change of the currency system, loans to various provinces to maintain financial lending have been spread out by several million yuan, so institutional loans have also increased considerably. As for valuable securities, since the increase in capital was resolved at the last general meeting of shareholders, the government allocated 11 million yuan of financial public bond par value in the 24th year to offset the official share item. The new and unpaid capital was actually invested with an increase of over 2,380,000 yuan, in addition to transferring 2 million yuan to the savings department as an increase in funds. In general, the bank's loans and investments this year do not favor any aspect. All those that can help production and improve finance will do their best according to their needs.

(4) Profit and Loss: The net profit of the bank in the 24th year was over 1,290,900 yuan, an increase of over 383,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 290,500 yuan compared to the 22nd year. Analyzing its content, interest and handling fees are still the main source of profit. The total revenue of profits was over 6,331,000 yuan, an increase of over 1,170,500 yuan compared to the previous year. As for the loss items, various expenses have increased slightly with the development of business, totaling over 3,619,000 yuan. Real estate and wealth were still allocated and withdrawn according to past precedents, totaling over 963,000 yuan. In addition, bad debts totaled over 137,000 yuan, and issuance tax totaled over 320,900 yuan. The total payment of losses was over 5,040,900 yuan. The net profit was over 1,290,900 yuan after offsetting profit and loss. This is the general situation of profit and loss this year.

3. Issuance and Preparation Situation

At the end of the 24th year, the total amount of banknotes in circulation in the bank, excluding nominal banknotes from Liaoning and Harbin and other old banknotes that were only received but not issued, was 180,825,650 yuan, an increase of 77,590,800 yuan compared with the total amount of banknotes in circulation at the end of the 23rd year. In terms of reserve funds, the cash reserve fund was 117,621,833 yuan, accounting for over 65% of the circulation amount. The guarantee reserve fund was 63,200,317 yuan, accounting for less than 35% of the circulation amount. In terms of the issuance situation throughout the year, although the off-season months of February, March, April, and May also saw a decline as in previous years, they were slightly higher than the same months in the 23rd year. After June, it gradually increased. By the end of October, it was equal to the highest amount at the end of the previous year. After the implementation of the new currency system in November, the amount of banknotes in circulation in the bank increased even more after being designated as legal tender.

4. Business Situation of the Savings Department

(1) Savings and Investments: The savings department of the bank originally had a fund of 500,000 yuan. This year, in order to expand the savings business, it increased the fund by 2 million yuan, for a total of 2.5 million yuan. The total balance of savings deposits was over 46,083,000 yuan, an increase of over 16,055,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 27,663,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. Among them, fixed savings deposits accounted for 63.9% of the total, and current savings deposits accounted for 36%. Compared with previous years, both fixed and current deposits have increased. However, the four northeastern provinces have stopped receiving new savings deposits due to environmental reasons, so the savings deposits in that area have been declining. Otherwise, the overall increase would be more than this. As for the use of savings deposits, the principle is still to strive for stability and comply with the Savings Bank Law. In total, the amount of loans and investments this year was over 19,450,000 yuan, excluding current deposits and loans, an increase of over 9,339,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 13,004,000 yuan compared to the 22nd year. The purchase of security bonds totaled over 12,451,000 yuan, which has exceeded one-quarter of the statutory savings total, an increase of over 6,512,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year. Mortgage loans totaled over 6,999,000 yuan, an increase of over 2,826,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year. Among them, real estate mortgage loans accounted for 18.7% of the total, security mortgage loans accounted for 57.5% of the total, and deposit certificate and passbook mortgage loans accounted for 23.8% of the total. This is the general situation.

(2) Profit and Loss: The net profit of the savings department of the bank in the 24th year was over 110,800 yuan, an increase of over 24,000 yuan compared to the 23rd year and an increase of over 30,400 yuan compared to the 22nd year. It is proposed to continue to roll over under the public accumulation item according to the precedents of previous years in order to increase the foundation. This is the general situation of profit and loss this year.

5. Rowing Affairs and Work Situation

Regarding the reform of rowing affairs and various tasks, this year we have made every effort to advance according to the established policy. The important ones are described below.

(1) Capital Increase and Reorganization: In March of this year, the government issued 100 million yuan of financial public bonds for the purpose of adjusting finance and maintaining industry and commerce, which were allocated to the bank, the Central Bank, and the Bank of China to increase share capital and other purposes. The bank was approved to revise the Traffic Bank Regulations according to the government order, and the total amount of the bank's share capital was changed to 20 million yuan of national currency, expanding the official share to 12 million yuan. The official share recognized by the government in the 17th year was also fully allocated with financial public bonds. All dividends, share rights, and director and supervisor quotas were revised. The bank was still granted a special license by the government to be a bank for developing national industries, and the types of business did not change significantly. It was still entrusted by the government to handle various affairs, and it could also be entrusted by the Central Bank to handle them. The bank's responsibilities were therefore more important, and its capital was doubled. As for the revised bank's articles of association, the shareholders' general meeting had already resolved and passed them in the previous session, and then they were submitted to the Ministry of Finance for revision, approval, and record.

(2) Adding Institutions: The bank's promotion of business in recent years has been based on assisting industry and balancing finance in urban and inland areas. The expansion of the business network is mainly along the coastline and the Longhai Line. The implementation situation has been detailed in the previous year's business report. This year's business is still based on the original policy and is working hard. The business institutions in Qin, Jin, Bian, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong have been continuously developed or adjusted. The branches and departments in Northeast China have also been reorganized separately or directly revoked in order to adapt to the times. Therefore, although the number of new branches, offices, and warehouses opened by the bank this year has increased to more than 30, the total number of existing branches and institutions has not far exceeded that of previous years. The increase or decrease of institutions is related to the expenses of the whole bank. It is necessary to pay equal attention to increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. The number of warehouses continued to increase this year. The newly opened ones include Hanyang, Changsha, Ningbo, Wuxi, Huangqiao, Qingjiangpu, Bengbu, and Suiyuan. Others are also under construction and preparation.

(3) Building Bank Houses and Warehouses: The modern economic environment is changing rapidly. Bank business houses and warehouses for storing mortgaged goods cannot be fully applied to leased houses. In addition to the new houses that the banks in Hankou, Harbin, Dalian, Yantai, etc. had built themselves, the houses of the Nanjing and Changshu branches and the Shanghai warehouse were also newly built and completed in the previous year. The bank houses under construction this year include four places, Zhenjiang, Changsha, Xuzhou, and Gulangyu. There are also five warehouses in Bengbu, Changsha, Ningbo, Xi'an, and Weinan. More than half of the construction has been completed, and there are more than one or two bases that have been purchased and are waiting for design and construction. In short, the construction of houses and the advancement of business are closely related and cannot be delayed.

(4) Assisting Industries: This year, from spring to autumn, domestic industries have been impacted by international financial policies and rural disasters. The dynamics of the industrial sector have gradually become active since the currency reform in early November. However, the purchasing power of the people has not increased, and the industry and commerce themselves still need to be enriched. All these situations have been described above. The bank's mission is to develop industries, and it should have appropriate assistance in this environment. In the past year, the bank has cooperated in the planned improvement of silkworms, the preparation and control of fisheries, and the regional management of agricultural loans. Among them, special attention has been paid to the expansion of export businesses. As for the industrial and commercial aspects, such as textile factories, flour factories, and chemical factories, if their business can be expected to advance, but they lack working capital and cannot expand their effectiveness, they will be given loans to facilitate turnover. For those with a large scope and large needs, who need to plan as a whole to be able to operate and promote, we will assist in the design to make them come up with a reasonable plan or issue corporate bonds entrusted by the bank to promote their ability to regenerate and complete the bank's mission of assisting and regulating. In terms of the bank's business policy, it is based on conservatism and seeks the safety of operations. In view of the fact that various industries in China are mostly emerging, and the operating efficiency may not be as expected, the bank also appoints staff to check at any time during the loan period, so as to seek to improve its efficiency in the regulation of the economy. This is not only to seek meticulous investment, but also the bank's high expectations for industry and commerce.

(5) Promoting Construction Projects: In recent years, the government has been bravely advancing construction projects. All the construction of railways and highways, the dredging of water conservancy dikes, etc., have been far-sighted and actively carried out. All the measures are the foundation for the restoration and economic foundation, and the bank has a long-standing relationship in its historical mission. In the past year, the bank has done its best to assist in the liaison of the Jiangnan Railway and the Jingwu Line, the extension of the West-Bao section of the Longhai Railway, the paving of the Xiangqian Highway, the dredging of the Huai River Project and the Yellow River Water Conservancy, etc., which the bank believes can improve people's livelihood and develop production. As for the projects that have not been completed before, such as the construction of the Qiantang River Bridge, the opening of the Weihe Diversion Canal, and the development of the Huainan Railway Coal Mine, etc., we will continue to assist according to the original proposal. Construction projects and the development of industries are closely related, and the bank's mission is to help.

(6) Regulating the Market: The state of the tense market situation after the start of the year has been described earlier. The bank, in view of the fact that the Shanghai financial market is the lifeline of the country and cannot be ignored, jointly made loans with the Central Bank and the Bank of China to various trading houses to facilitate turnover, and purchased silver from Hong Kong and London to help alleviate the temporary panic in the market. When the market was tight again in the summer, the government took emergency relief measures, and the bank also joined colleagues to form a syndicate to carry out lending, and jointly with the Bank of China to serve as the central exchange for foreign exchange instruments, and tried its best to adjust for various trading houses to barely survive the crisis. Starting in August, the bank and its colleagues jointly organized industrial and commercial loans for more general regulation. All these are only temporary measures to adapt to the environment, but at the time of extremely tight money, the room for maneuver was effective. After the implementation of the new currency system, the bank's banknotes were designated as legal tender, and the society had higher expectations for the bank. The bank also followed the government's policy and weighed the surplus and deficit of local market conditions at any time, and gave adjustments to help the implementation of the currency system and establish a solid foundation.

(7) Expanding Trust Business: The bank's trust business has previously handled service-oriented businesses such as custody of securities, agency insurance, and property management. This year, in view of the increasing need for trust business in society and the important relationship between trust business and the bank's special mission of developing industries, the bank has specially formulated trust regulations and submitted them to the ministry for record. The trust fund is also intended to be allocated separately and operated independently to ensure security. The rules for various trust businesses have also been formulated separately with reference to the systems of various countries, and the implementation will be decided on a case-by-case basis depending on the needs of the location of each branch.

(8) Personnel Improvement: Since the bank's business has gradually developed, all personnel facilities must be improved to increase efficiency. This year, the policy on personnel measures, in addition to continuing to use the examination system for recruiting personnel, and strictly screening the existing employees, also separately formulated retirement measures. The special attention is paid to: (1) accounting training. All the special probationary employees recruited last year and the original employees who still lack sufficient experience in accounting affairs will be placed in a specially established accounting training class. All accounting affairs, from vouchers to final accounts, will be guided item by item to become familiar with them. After the training period expires, they will be sent to branches for practice so that they can become proficient in practical techniques. (2) Factory internships. The bank believes that factory loans should first understand the content of the factory. Therefore, when selecting graduates from various universities as special probationary employees last year, it has paid attention to the cultivation of specialized academics. This year, it has taken a further step to specially select and send special probationary employees to cement, paper, acid, and textile factories to investigate the machinery and equipment, manufacturing costs, and product sales of each factory. It is important to pay attention to on-site practice. It has now been completed one after another, and these special probationary employees will be assigned to various positions. (3) Enriching library facilities. Modern bank employees, in addition to the corresponding skills, also rely on peacetime cultivation to enrich their knowledge. For special affairs, it is indispensable to have various books for reference. The bank's library facilities are based on this purpose. This year, it has continued to add to the storage of books, which are classified and stored according to the new classification method. From now on, it will not be difficult to become a great view over the years.

The above-mentioned points are of great importance to the development of the bank's business. Now that they have been implemented in order, the results can be expected. However, the economic business is changing with each passing day, and the bank's business must seek to advance with the times. The achievements in the past period should not be self-painted by the bank.

6. Future Efforts

The reason why the domestic economic business is declining is that, in short, there are only two reasons: financial tightness and stagnation of production and sales. Therefore, if we want to assist agriculture, industry, and commerce to restore their purpose today, it lies in cultivating the production function. The means are tied to the turnover of finance in various industries. The methods of turning over finance in various industries, those related to direct action are the lending of funds, such as agricultural, industrial, and commercial loans. Those related to indirect action are the promotion of business, such as increasing business institutions and goods warehouses. Although the two methods are different, the promotion of business is nothing more than the use of funds to facilitate the promotion of agriculture, industry, and commerce. The bank's past business and work situation have paid attention to the above two points. The direction of future efforts is also here. Let's analyze it.

(1) Pay attention to remortgaging to regulate the market and finance. Mortgage is a method of financing funds, which is slightly similar to discounting, but the term is different. Discounted bills are shorter in term and must be supported by rediscounting. Mortgage loans are longer in term and must be remortgaged to finance their turnover. The so-called remortgaging means that one party's mortgage debt is remortgaged to the other party. Today, the biggest difficulty in the economic circle is the stagnation of book debt, and the resources that can help each other are very limited. Now, if we want to make full use of this limited mutual assistance resources to avoid the stagnation of book mortgage debt, in addition to discounting, we have to organize remortgaging according to the method of rediscounting to fill the credit market and promote financial turnover. This is the first point.

(2) Pay attention to corporate bonds to support the cow production business. The advantage of remortgaging to industrial and commercial finance is as described above. A further step is the fundraising of corporate bonds, which is the main way to enlighten social enterprise investment. The bank's revised regulations originally stipulated that the management, subscription, or acceptance of corporate bonds should be one of the business operations. There are more than one or two who are now agreeing to undertake the operation. In the future, we should further promote it according to the needs of the society to promote social enterprise investment. However, the bank's investment should be limited to production businesses. We should still study the organization, management, equipment, and cost of the company in detail to ensure that the investment is not in vain and the matter is practical, and the purpose of assisting production is completed. This is the second point.

(3) Support exporters to adjust foreign trade.

The above two points mainly focus on the circulation of finance to help the production and sales of goods. However, the effectiveness of financial circulation must be sought to circulate domestically without flowing out to foreign countries. Therefore, supporting the production and sales of goods should focus on domestic agricultural and industrial products. For export commodities such as silk and cotton, tea, and mineral products, we should use various methods to help promote them so that export trade can be smoothly transferred and production and sales businesses can be increased accordingly.
